- [x] **Cycle 0099 — Auth screen redesign (dual-shape cinematic, dark)** ✅ shipped 2026-05-05 (14 commits, ddc04ff → ac1fcff). Plan `plans/0099-auth-redesign.md`. Auth había quedado en plain-HTML detrás del overhaul; este cycle lo trae al nivel del resto. **Dos layouts intencionalmente distintos** seleccionados via `matchMedia(max-width: 1023px)`:
  - **L (≥1024px)** — full-bleed `<picture>` hero (AVIF + WebP, format negotiation), radial scrim, `wordmark` fijo top-left (60 px) como brand anchor, columna izquierda (left:56, bottom:56, width:420) con stack pitch + glass card + footer-extracted, glass card en `color-mix(--sp-bg-2 88%, transparent) + backdrop-filter blur(14px)` + border-soft + shadow-lg + radius-lg, **right pitch** "Every character has a heartbeat." con `right:56, bottom:80, max-width:460, text-align:right` — bottom edge alineado pixel-perfect con el bottom del card (delta=0), terms + © como elemento abs separado al pie del column. Imagen `frontend/public/images/auth-hero.{avif,webp}` (creador la generó con Seedream prompt cosmic-vortex).
  - **S (<1024px)** — image area `flex:0 0 42vh` (sin max-width frame; intentos de capear el layout entero produjeron dark gutters laterales feos) + sheet sólida bg-2 con `border-top:1px solid border-soft` (hairline para el seam, sin box-shadow) + `border-radius-xl` top + `marginTop:-20` para overlap con el gradient bottom de la imagen. **Contenido centrado con max-width** dentro de cada zona: brand pitch overlay max-width 460 + 24 px padding, form sheet `align-items:center` con inner wrapper max-width 420. Logo S: 44 px + drop-shadow + 20 px de breathing room antes del chip.
  - **State machine 100% preservada**: `mode` / `email` / `password` / `submitting` / `error` / `notice` / `recovering` tri-state ("resolving" guard intacto), `withBusy` / `onEmailSubmit`, anon→upgrade flow (`linkIdentity` + `updateUser`).
  - **OAuth state**: GitHub button removido por completo. Google button visible pero disabled con copy "Continue with Google · soon" + cursor:not-allowed + opacity 0.65 — re-habilitar quitando `disabled` cuando provider esté wireado en Supabase. Helper `onOAuth` y `Provider` import borrados; re-añadir cuando se reactive.
  - **Inputs**: `box-sizing:border-box` en input/primary/ghost styles — sin esto `width:100%` overflows el card right edge por +28 px (border + padding) → el bug se vio live antes de bloquearlo.
  - **Wordmark proporciones**: `align-self:flex-start + flex-shrink:0` en el `<img>` — sin esto el flex column padre forzaba `align-items:stretch` y deformaba el aspect ratio del PNG (3.42 → 10.45 al renderizar 460×44 sobre nativo 684×200).
  - **MessageImage observer dep fix paralelo**: durante el live test de cycle 0099 se descubrió que `useEffect` deps `[inView]` solamente provocaban que el IntersectionObserver no se reconectara al cambiar de variant (fixe en commit del cycle 0099 paralelo); deps ahora `[inView, image?.id, image?.sfw_blocked]`.
  - **testIDs**: `auth-shell-l` / `auth-shell-s` / `auth-brand-pitch` / `auth-side-pitch` / `auth-error` / `auth-oauth-google` / `auth-forgot-link` / `signin-submit` / `signup-submit` / `reset-submit`. tsc 0 errors. Verificado live a 1440×900 (L), 1004×774 (S intermedio), 430×932 (iPhone 14 Pro Max).

- [x] **Cycle 0100 — Brand re-paint: amber signature + neutral surfaces + dark-text-on-amber** ✅ shipped 2026-05-06 (5 commits: `6f6da4a` → `5d1bdef` → `12b8c7c` → `3809e67`, plus `6123b72` handoff). Multi-step rebrand to break visual association with PersonaLLM. Final state of all token changes:
  - **Brand gradient**: violet `#8B5CF6` + teal `#34D399` → **amber `#F5B547` + sunset `#FF7B3D`** at 135deg. Why amber: the auth-hero image already had amber as the dominant warm bloom — the brand visual was in the content, just not in tokens. Differentiates vs PersonaLLM and vs Character.ai blue / Replika rose / Janitor purple / Spicychat pink. Lamp-light / parchment / sunset semantic fit for a story-craft product.
  - **Surface palette neutralized**: bg/borders shifted from violet-tinted to balanced neutral grays. `--sp-bg #0D0A15 → #0F0F10`, `bg-1 → #161617`, `bg-2 → #1C1C1E`, `bg-3 → #252527`, `bg-inset → #0A0A0B`, plus matching neutral border-soft/border/border-strong (`#202022 / #2B2B2D / #3A3A3D`). Luminance preserved within ±1 so elevation hierarchy still reads. Result: chrome reads as plain dark gray with amber as the only chromatic signature.
  - **`--char-accent` default**: was `var(--sp-accent-violet)` → now `var(--sp-brand-1)` (amber). Sidebar nav active state and the Settings footer button used `var(--char-accent-soft)` which leaked violet into otherwise-neutralized chrome when no character was loaded; default now amber so on-brand. Per-character chat scope still overrides via inline style on the chat root.
  - **Section titles white**: the `.sp-wordmark` CSS class (page H1 heading on Settings, Gallery, Recent Characters, etc.) was rendering text via the brand gradient (`background-clip:text`). Now solid `var(--sp-fg)`. White section titles match the white-glow logo PNG; amber stays reserved for action surfaces only. Brand voice: white = identity / hierarchy, amber = action.
  - **Dark text on amber buttons**: white text on warm amber gradient was barely legible. New token **`--sp-fg-on-brand: #000000`** (pure black, sharper contrast than `--sp-bg`'s near-black). Applied across 14 button surfaces — AuthForm primary, panelStyles (chat regen/fork/image-gen), Composer send, CharacterForm save + active tab pill, Profile save, and 8 settings pages (Text/Memory/Visual/Image/Grammar/Memory/WritingStyles/TTS) for both primary buttons AND active toggle tabs. Avatar initial bubbles (white text on per-character accent bg) intentionally untouched — those are character identity surfaces, not brand surfaces.
  - **Final cromatic system**: white = identity (logo, page titles, body); amber gradient = primary action bg (Sign in, Save, Send, Generate); amber solid `--sp-brand-1` = links / chips / focus / sidebar active tint; pure-black `--sp-fg-on-brand` = text on amber surfaces; neutral grays = chrome surfaces; per-character accents = chat scope only; status (destructive red / warning amber / success green) = functional, untouched.
  - **NO se cambió** (intencional): per-character accent system (16 presets + custom), status colors, the wordmark PNG asset itself.

- [x] **Cycle 0101 — Shell layout: inset content card + transparent sidebar** ✅ shipped 2026-05-06 (commit `48100a2`). Plan `plans/0101-shell-inset-card-layout.md`. Lift estructural del kit `ui-prototype-traveliru-partners/ui_kits/index.html` (función `renderScreen`, líneas 459–482) adaptado a tokens dark de StoryPlots:
  - **Outer wrapper**: bg unified (`--sp-bg`), no se ve diferencia entre el área de la sidebar y el resto de la página.
  - **Sidebar (`Sidebar.tsx`)**: `background: transparent`, sin `border-right`. Visualmente se funde con el outer bg — no se siente un panel diferenciado, sino parte del fondo. Width igual: 280 expanded / 64 collapsed.
  - **Content card** (en `AppShell.tsx`): el wrapper que contiene topbar + `<Outlet>` ahora se estiliza como card flotante en el L breakpoint — `margin: "16px 16px 16px 0"` (no margin-left porque pega a la sidebar), `background: --sp-bg-2`, `border-radius: --sp-radius-lg`, `box-shadow: --sp-shadow-sm`, `overflow: hidden`. En non-persistent (S/M, drawer mode) la card se aplana a full-bleed (sin margin/radius/shadow) porque no hay sidebar para enmarcarla. El doble-scroll riesgo se mitiga así: card es `overflow:hidden`, el inner outlet wrapper mantiene `overflow: outletOverflow` (auto para static routes, hidden para `/chat/*`).
  - **Logo dual** (en Sidebar header): expanded muestra `/logos/logo.png` a `height:40` + tagline "Step into stories". Collapsed muestra el mismo PNG a `max-width:40 height:auto` (~12 px alto). El header en collapsed pasa a `flex-direction: column` con gap, así el wordmark y el botón de expand-arrow se apilan verticalmente en lugar de pelearse el ancho del 64 px sidebar. **Pending**: el creador subirá un asset dedicado mark-only en `frontend/public/logos/logo-mark.{png,svg}` (mencionó `Logo2.png` como candidato — sin trackear todavía); cuando llegue, swap el `src` en Sidebar.tsx ~línea 91.
  - **RecentChats colapsado** (`RecentChats.tsx`): nueva prop `collapsed: boolean`. Cuando true renderiza columna vertical de avatars 32×32 (sin label, sin nombres, sin snippets). Cada avatar mantiene el `<Link>` a su conversation con `title` para tooltip y `box-shadow` con el accent del char. El Skeleton también tiene variant collapsed. Sidebar pasa el state a través.
  - **testIDs preservados**: `sidebar`, `sidebar-backdrop`, `sidebar-hamburger`, `sidebar-collapse`, `recent-chats`, `recent-{conversation_id}`, todos los `nav-*`. Drawer mode (mobile) intacto.
  - **Open follow-up único**: dedicated logo-mark asset para reemplazar el wordmark scaled-down en collapsed state.

- [x] **Cycle 0102 — Visual chrome consistency pass: borders + radii + chat surfaces + settings flow** ✅ shipped 2026-05-06 (uncommitted al momento del handoff). Sin plan formal — barrido de polish guiado por feedback iterativo del creator post-0101. Cubre **9 changes**, todos contained al frontend (cero backend / DB / non-negotiable touched):
  - **(A) Border tokens cascade bump** (`frontend/src/styles/tokens.css:36-43`) — `--sp-border` `#2B2B2D → #52525B` (luma 43→88), `--sp-border-soft` `#202022 → #3F3F46` (32→63), `--sp-border-strong` `#3A3A3D → #71717A` (58→127). Razón: los borders estaban a luma casi-igual al bg-2 (#1C1C1E luma 28), produciendo el efecto "carved/inset" en outlined surfaces (ghost pills, fieldsets). Fix cascada — afecta los 106 call sites del token sin patching per-component. Token-only change, una línea de revert si algo queda chunky.
  - **(B) Sidebar dividers removed** (`Sidebar.tsx:75,167` + `RecentChats.tsx:112,160,221,234`) — 6 hairlines `borderTop/borderBottom: 1px solid --sp-border` quitadas (debajo del brand header, encima del Settings/Sign out footer, y los 4 separators del Recent Chats en sus 4 estados — collapsed/expanded/skeleton/skeleton-collapsed). El sidebar ahora fluye como una sola columna separada solo por whitespace. Padding del footer bumped `0.5rem → 0.75rem` para compensar la pérdida visual del divider. Sentía "anticuado" con los rectángulos apilados.
  - **(C) Settings sub-pages estandarizados** — los 10 routes (`DataSecuritySettings`, `PromptEditor`, `WritingStylesSettings`, `ImageEngineSettings`, `TextToSpeechSettings`, `TextEngineSettings`, `GrammarSettings`, `MemoryEngineSettings`, `MemorySettings`, `VisualRoleplaySettings`) homogeneizados a `maxWidth: 640, margin: "2rem auto", padding: "0 1rem"`. Antes había 3 valores (560, 640, 720) + Grammar como outlier (560 + 1.5rem). El intermedio 640 elimina el "Grammar es muy alto y los otros muy cortos" feedback.
  - **(D) Chat surfaces re-skin** (`MessageBubble.tsx:123-146,306-323` + `MessageAudioButton.tsx:161-175`) — tres pisos:
    - **User bubble**: `bg: var(--char-accent)` flat → `linear-gradient(135deg, var(--char-accent) 0%, color-mix(in oklab, var(--char-accent) 80%, black) 100%)` — efecto "lit dome", suaviza el solid fill que con accents shade-600/700 (cycle 0072 ACCENT_PRESETS) leía demasiado loud.
    - **Assistant bubble**: `bg: --sp-bg-2` (= panel surface del AppShell, invisible) → `bg: --sp-bg-3`. Border `transparent` → `1px solid --sp-border-soft` siempre (no solo cuando `hasManyVariants`). Resultado: bubble visible como card sobre el panel del chat.
    - **ActionRail chips (↻/⑂/🖼/▶)**: era `bg: --char-accent-soft + border: --char-accent + color: --char-accent` (toda la chip teñida del accent del character → fatiga visual). Ahora `bg: --sp-bg-3 + border: --sp-border-soft + color: --char-accent`. El accent vive solo en el icono, el frame es neutro consistente con el assistant bubble. Mismo patrón aplicado en `MessageAudioButton.tsx` para que los 4 chips (regenerate / fork / generate-image / play-audio) sean idénticos.
  - **(E) One Radius migration** — colapso del scale de radii a 3 formas únicas en todo el sistema. Token file (`frontend/src/styles/tokens.css:137-144`): de 5 vars (`--sp-radius-{sm:8, md:10, lg:14, xl:20, pill:999}`) a 2 (`--sp-radius: 14px` + `--sp-radius-pill: 999px`). Sweep masivo via sed across ~45 files: todos los `var(--sp-radius-{sm,md,lg,xl,pill})` → `var(--sp-radius)`, todos los literales `borderRadius: {4,6,8,12,14,18,22,999}` → `var(--sp-radius)`. **Distribución final**: 141 sitios `var(--sp-radius)` (14px — buttons, inputs, cards, panels, modals, bubbles, tabs, sectionCards, dropdowns, composer), 29 sitios `50%` (avatars + action chips, los únicos casos donde la forma ES redonda), 4 sitios `999px` (scrollbar thumb, `.sp-toggle` track, `.sp-range` track, `.sp-range::-moz-range-progress` — semantic pills exclusivamente). Cambios visibles más perceptibles: composer `22 → 14`, user bubble `18 → 14`, ghost pills (Upload image, Generate Avatar, Save, Cancel) y tabs Avatar/Info/Settings outer container `999 → 14`. **Diseño signature**: 14px es el radio elegido — entre Linear/GitHub (8, utility) y consumer apps (20+, casual), creando una identidad propia distinta a PersonaLLM (pill-everywhere) sin ser sharp/utility. tsc 0 errors post-sweep.
  - **(F) Edit Character — "Back" link → X icon + smart return** (`CharacterForm.tsx:1-15,415-440`) — el header del Edit Character tenía `<Link to="/characters">Back</Link>`. Reemplazado por `<button>` con `<Icon icon={X} size={18} />` (Lucide). Nueva async `handleClose`: si `editing && character && userId`, hace `loadPersona() + findOrCreateForCharacter()` y navega a `/chat/<charId>/<convId>` (vuelve al chat del character — preserva contexto conversacional); else (new character o error) navega a `/characters`. Imports añadidos: `X` (lucide-react), `Icon` (lib/Icon), `findOrCreateForCharacter` (lib/conversations). Botón con `var(--sp-radius)` border-only ghost 36×36, `--sp-border` border + `--sp-fg-2` color. Testid nuevo: `character-form-close`. Era un dolor de UX: editar el character desde un chat te tiraba de vuelta a `/characters` en vez de seguir conversando.
  - **(G) Chat header — back button removido** (`ChatShell.tsx:2,581-587`) — quitado el `<Link to="/characters">` con `ArrowLeft` que estaba a la izquierda del avatar+nombre del character. Frees ~40px de header space. Cleanup del import `ArrowLeft` (no quedaron consumers). Para volver a `/characters` sigue estando la nav del sidebar (siempre visible), y el avatar+nombre del header siguen siendo `<Link>` a `/character/<id>/edit`. Creator: "no se usa mucho ese botón".
  - **(H) Composer send button — neutral ghost** (`Composer.tsx:75-80`) — el send button (↑) era `bg: var(--sp-brand-grad)` amber gradient cuando enabled. Pero el chat es el espacio del *character*, no de StoryPlots — el amber peleaba con el accent del user bubble (que es del char, gradient a color-mix). Ahora: `bg: var(--sp-bg-3)` constante (enabled y disabled), `border: --sp-border` (enabled) o `--sp-border-soft` (disabled), `color: --sp-fg` (enabled) o `--sp-fg-4` (disabled). El cambio active→disabled se transmite por brillo de border + icono, no por color de marca. Brand amber reservado para CTAs de marca (Save, Sign in, Enrich-with-AI).
  - **(I) Settings on L auto-redirect** (`SettingsLayout.tsx`) — entrar a `/settings` en desktop (`bp === "L"`) mostraba `<div data-testid="settings-empty-pane">Select a section to view its settings.</div>` — pantalla muerta. Ahora `<Navigate to="/settings/prompt-editor" replace />` cuando `isIndex && bp === "L"`. El `replace` evita loop con el back del browser. Mobile (S/M) intacto — el drill-through del picker sigue siendo el right move ahí. Removido el placeholder div + testid `settings-empty-pane`.
  - **Verificación**: tsc 0 errors después de cada change. TS check ejecutado entre micro-changes (5+ veces). Visual verification pendiente — el creator confirmó OK el batch (D), (E) post-cascada-borders, (G), (H), (I) en vivo durante la sesión; (A)+(B)+(C)+(F) confirmados visualmente vía screenshots compartidos. Playwright run formal no se hizo en esta sesión (changes contained al chrome, no behavior). Si algo regrede, candidatos a investigar: ghost pills muy "boxy" sin pill, user bubble pierde shape distinctiva, scrollbar thumb (uses `--sp-border-strong` = nuevo `#71717A`) puede sentirse chunky.
  - **Tokens en estado final** (`tokens.css`):
    - Borders: `--sp-border: #52525B; --sp-border-soft: #3F3F46; --sp-border-strong: #71717A;`
    - Radii: `--sp-radius: 14px; --sp-radius-pill: 999px;`
  - **Open follow-up declarado por creator antes de cerrar la sesión**: cambios al sidebar (próxima sesión).

- [x] **Cycle 0103 — Sidebar redesign (footer cluster + auto-collapse + floating toggle)** ✅ shipped 2026-05-06 (commit `4ff52f8`). Sin plan formal — feedback-driven post-0102 sidebar polish. **Footer reordenado a Persona → Settings → Sign out** (cycle también probó Settings → Persona → Sign out, descartado). YourPersonaCard sale del top scrollable, **3 footer rows uniformes** (mismo `itemStyle`-style shape; Persona conserva avatar+text, Settings/Sign out icon+label). **Sign out visible en collapsed**: `UserSection.tsx` refactorizada para aceptar `collapsed: boolean`; signed-in renderiza `LogOut` icon + label; anonymous/signed-out → `LogIn` + `UserPlus` con CTAs en expanded. Email span removido. **Auto-collapse on nav click**: `AppShell.handleNavClick` setea `collapsed=true` + persiste vía `saveSidebarCollapsed`. Wired a todos los nav rows (Home/Characters/Gallery/Grammar/Settings/Persona/Sign out). **Floating chevron control**: extraído del header, render absoluto en sibling-of-header (`right: -12, top: 14, z-index: 5`) — sticks 12px past sidebar edge into content gutter (Traveliru pattern). Mismo position en ambos states (collapsed+expanded) para muscle memory. **Active state margin**: `itemStyle.margin: collapsed ? "0 4px" : "0 0.5rem"` para que el active fill no toque sidebar edges. **Settings drops el `settingsBtnStyle`** especial → ahora usa `itemStyle` igual que primary nav (consistencia total).

- [x] **Cycle 0104 — Mobile sheet pattern + sidebar polish iteration + chat overlay panels + auth contrast + recent-chats active state** ✅ shipped 2026-05-06 (uncommitted al momento del handoff). Sin plan formal — barrido extenso de polish iterativo guiado por creator feedback. Cubre **~12 changes** distribuidos en chrome layouts, sidebar, chat, panels, auth y character chrome. Todos contained al frontend (cero backend / DB / non-negotiable touched).
  - **(A) Mobile sheet pattern para AppShell + ChatShell.** El user noticed que mobile no tenía el "lifted card" feel del desktop (cycle 0101). Iteración multi-step que terminó en patrón híbrido limpio:
    - **AppShell topbar (mobile non-chat)**: `position: relative` (en flow), bg gradient `linear-gradient(180deg, var(--sp-bg) 0%, var(--sp-bg) 55%, var(--sp-bg-2) 100%)` — solid page-bg al top (Safari address bar extends seamlessly) → bg-2 al bottom. Sin `pointer-events: none`, sin `backdrop-filter` (intentamos overlay con blur, hacía que content scrolleado desapareciera bajo solid portion + line visible al cut). Reverted a in-flow.
    - **AppShell content card (mobile non-chat)**: bg-2 sin radius (las rounded corners creaban "mini cut" perceptible). **Sticky fade strip** a `top: 0, height: 28, marginBottom: -28, zIndex: 1, pointerEvents: none` con `linear-gradient(180deg, var(--sp-bg-2) 0%, transparent 100%)` — disuelve el topmost 28px del contenido conforme scrollea, sin overlay weirdness.
    - **ChatShell header mobile**: bg gradient `var(--sp-bg) → var(--sp-bg) 70% → var(--sp-bg-2)` (más solid extendido que el AppShell topbar para más zona dark prominente — el user lo pidió tras ver versión inicial 55%). Padding mobile bumped a `20px 12px 14px` (vs `10px 12px` desktop) para dar la presencia de zona dark del Settings/Home topbar. Desktop conserva `bg-1` (cycle 0067 hairline pattern) actualizado a transparent + hairline para integrarse al AppShell card.
    - **ChatShell content area (mobile)**: bg-2 sin radius, `position: relative`, **absolute fade overlay top 28px** mismo gradient pattern que AppShell.
    - **Composer**: removido `borderTop: 1px solid --sp-border-soft` y `background: --sp-bg-1`. Hereda bg del padre (chat surface bg-2). El input pill mismo carries the visual definition; ya no hay chrome footer alrededor.
  - **(B) Token nuevo `--sp-radius-sheet: 20px`.** Para iOS-style sheet top corners en auth + content card mobile + chat content (cuando aplicaba). El value pasó de 14 → 20 para más "sheet feel" iOS. Después al final del cycle eliminamos las rounded corners del AppShell content card mobile (los corners creaban un cut visible) — el token sigue disponible y aplica solo a `AuthForm.tsx` (auth bottom sheet).
  - **(C) ChatControlsPanel + GrammarSidebarPanel siempre overlay (mobile + desktop).** Removido el `inline` mode del desktop — el inline panel cortaba el chat content visualmente. Ahora ambos render como side-drawer overlay 360px desde la derecha, **mismo pattern en ambos breakpoints**. `inspectorMode: "modal"` constante. Bloque `controlsOpen && inspectorMode === "inline"` removido (dead code post-change). **GrammarSidebarPanel overlayPanelStyle restructurado**: era `inset: 0` (full page) → ahora `top:0, right:0, bottom:0, width: 360, maxWidth: 100%` (right-docked match con ChatControlsPanel). Ambos paneles con `boxShadow: "-12px 0 32px rgba(0,0,0,0.4)"` para softening del border-left contra el backdrop. **Scroll fix**: ambos paneles tenían `height: 100%` que no resolvía bien dentro del flex parent → cambiado a `height: 100vh, maxHeight: 100vh, minHeight: 0` + `display: flex, flexDirection: column` (ChatControlsPanel) para que `overflowY: auto` engage cuando contenido excede viewport.
  - **(D) Sidebar polish iteration (post-0103).** Múltiples micro-cambios sobre cycle 0103:
    - **Logo asset swap**: collapsed mode usa `/logos/logo-reduced.png` (square 36×36 SP mark) en vez de wordmark scaled-down. Asset nuevo trackeado.
    - **Auto-collapse on nav click REVERTED**: cycle 0103 lo introdujo, user lo rechazó porque "en pantallas grandes no tiene sentido". Removida `handleNavClick` de AppShell, removida prop `onNavClick` del Sidebar persistent, derivation simplificada a `props.mode === "drawer" ? props.onClose : undefined`.
    - **Persona avatar bg**: iteró por `--sp-brand-1` amber (rejected — too loud) → `--sp-bg-3` (rejected — barely visible) → `--sp-border-strong` (rejected — too light) → **`--sp-border`** final (luma ~88, mid-gray clearly visible without competing). Aplicado tanto en `YourPersonaCard.tsx` (expanded) como `CollapsedUserAvatar.tsx` (collapsed).
    - **Persona avatar size unified to 32×32** en ambos states (matches RecentChats avatars para columna visual continua). `boxShadow` removido del expanded (creaba ring dark contra el card bg que leía como negro llamativo).
    - **YourPersonaCard chrome**: del original heavy card `bg-2 + border` → ghost row transparent + active state `bg-3` cuando en `/profile` (vía `useMatch("/profile")`) → final con `border: 1px solid var(--sp-border)` (sin bg fill) — actua como visual divider entre Recent Chats arriba y Settings/Sign out abajo, accent color del border match al collapse-toggle button.
    - **Footer wrapper gap**: `0.25rem` → `0.5rem` (más breathing entre Persona / Settings / Sign out, especialmente cuando Settings selected).
    - **Sign out icon color**: `--sp-fg-2` → `--sp-fg` para compensar densidad visual de Lucide LogOut (menos strokes que el Settings gear).
    - **Brand header logo alignment**: expanded → left-aligned (`alignItems: flex-start, justifyContent: flex-start`, padding-left 1rem); collapsed → centered (`justifyContent: center`, padding simétrico).
    - **Chevron control rediseñado de cero múltiples veces**: el final pattern es `controlStyle("corner")` = top-right inside (24×24, top:24 right:14) para expanded + drawer, vs `controlStyle("below-logo")` = horizontally centered debajo del logo (18×18, top:60 left:50% transform translateX(-50%)) para collapsed. Brand header collapsed `minHeight: 84` para garantizar 28px buffer entre logo + chevron y entre chevron + first nav row.
    - **Chat pseudo-nav-item removed**: el bloque `{isChatActive && <div nav-chat-active>}` con icono MessageCircle eliminado. La distinción del chat activo migra a Recent Chats avatar (ver punto E).
  - **(E) Recent Chats active state.** Reemplaza el chat pseudo-nav-item removido. `useMatch("/chat/:characterId/:conversationId")` extrae el conversationId activo. Para cada row: `isActive = conv.id === activeConvId`. Visual:
    - **Expanded**: row sin bg fill (intentamos `bg: --sp-bg-3` pero leía heavy + competía con el avatar), conserva ring 3px del accent del char + adds **`boxShadow: 0 0 14px 2px ${accent}` glow halo** sobre el avatar — el active chat "pulsa" visualmente con el color del char.
    - **Collapsed**: ring del accent bumped 3px → 5px + glow halo. El avatar es lo único visible en collapsed, así que el active state se carga por completo en él.
    - `aria-current="page"` + `data-active="true"` en el Link para a11y / testing.
  - **(F) CharacterCard border neutralizado.** `var(--char-accent-border)` → `var(--sp-border)` neutral. El user noticed que con grid de characters multi-color, cada card pintaba un border diferente y leía como ruido. Identidad del char queda en el avatar ring (`boxShadow: 0 0 0 3px --char-accent`) que ya estaba.
  - **(G) Edit Character X close button refinado.**
    - In-form X (`CharacterForm.tsx`): removido `border` + `borderRadius` (ghost limpio sin chrome). Icon size 18 → 20. Solo visible en desktop (header `sp-main-header` sigue oculto en mobile via `tokens.css`).
    - **Mobile X moved to AppShell topbar**: `AppShell.tsx` agrega un nuevo conditional para `/character/` paths que renderiza X 36×36 a la derecha del topbar (mismo placement que el back arrow del settings sub-routes), `onClick: navigate(-1)` (browser back: chat o /characters según procedencia). Imports añadidos: `X` lucide, `useNavigate`. Testid `topbar-character-close`.
    - **AppShell topbar back arrow**: el conditional para `/character/` paths fue removido (cycle 0102 ya lo había removido para chat header, ahora también desde mobile topbar).
  - **(H) ConversationSwitcher mobile compact: borderless.** El `toggleBaseStyle` tenía `border: 1px solid --sp-border` permanente. En mobile compact (icon-only) sobreescrito a `border: 1px solid transparent` para match con los otros header icon buttons (Keyboard / Pencil / More). Desktop expanded (con texto + ▾) conserva el border.
  - **(I) AppShell topbar gradient + Mobile Settings auto-redirect.** Topbar mobile bg: gradient solid → bg-2 (resuelve el cut color). En desktop persistent, sigue intacto cycle 0101 (4-corner card). Plus AppShell auto-redirige `/settings` exact path a `/settings/prompt-editor` cuando bp === "L" (cycle 0102 ya tenía esto, sigue activo).
  - **(J) Settings on chat: auto-collapse trade-off resolved**. Por eso los chat panels van overlay siempre — eliminamos la necesidad de implementar el "auto-collapse left sidebar when right panel opens at medium widths" (cycle 0102/0103 backlog). Overlay pattern es siempre el mismo y no compite por horizontal space.
  - **(K) Auth screen contrast + Safari integration.**
    - **Mobile compact**: hero gradient overlay simplificado a `linear-gradient(180deg, var(--sp-bg) 0%, transparent 8%)` solo top fade (Safari address bar match). Bottom fade a bg-2 removido (era el original cycle 0099) — el sheet card abajo con su radius hace el cut visual.
    - **Desktop wide**: vignette radial intermedio `0.08 → 0.35 → 0.65` (probamos heavy original `0.15/0.55/0.85` y light `0/0.18/0.45`, intermedio se mejor). Plus stack adicional con top fade `linear-gradient(180deg, var(--sp-bg) 0%, transparent 5%)` — Safari address bar match.
    - **brandPitch text-shadow**: dual-layer `0 1px 3px rgba(0,0,0,0.9), 0 4px 24px rgba(0,0,0,0.7)` (sharp + soft halo, replaces single blur cycle 0099 que no rendía bien sobre brightest mid-zones del cosmic vortex).
    - **Sub copy color**: `--sp-fg-1` con `opacity: 0.95` → `--sp-fg` solid (text-shadow del parent ya levanta el texto, color full white restaura contraste).
  - **Verificación**: tsc 0 errors después de cada change. TS check ejecutado entre micro-changes (~15+ veces). Visual confirmation iterativa — múltiples screenshots del creator entre cambios resolvieron variantes (gradient stops del topbar, vignette intensity del auth, persona avatar bg color, chevron position en collapsed). **Lección aprendida**: siempre recordar que `min-height: 0` es necesario en flex/grid children con `overflow: auto` para que el scroll engage (caso del ChatControlsPanel scroll bug).
  - **Tokens en estado final** (`tokens.css`):
    - `--sp-radius-sheet: 20px` (NUEVO) — auth bottom sheet only (mobile content card y chat content perdieron las rounded corners durante iteración).
    - Resto de borders + radii igual al cycle 0102.
  - **Open follow-ups declarados por creator**: ninguno explícito al cierre de la sesión más allá de continuar polish.

- [x] **Cycle 0105 — v0.2 release prep + initial public deploy (Vercel + Render + Cloudflare)** ✅ shipped 2026-05-06 (commits `b3d0a99` → `1d0fadf` → `de56af6` → `732261d` → `b50d7d9` → `cbac89c`, tag `v0.2.0`).   - **(A) Favicons + SEO + custom-domain prep (commit `b3d0a99`).** Set completo de favicons movido de `frontend/` raíz a `frontend/public/` (Vite sólo sirve estáticos desde `public/`): `apple-touch-icon.png`, `favicon-96x96.png`, `favicon.ico`, `favicon.svg`, `web-app-manifest-192x192.png`, `web-app-manifest-512x512.png`, `site.webmanifest`. Hero "Every character has a heartbeat" preservado tras feedback creator. **Iteración de copy**: el creator descartó 3+ propuestas previas (incluyendo "Practice English by chatting with AI characters", "Every character remembers", "One character. GitHub mantiene auto-redirect del nombre viejo al nuevo. Local: `git remote set-url origin https://github.com/michael-v17/storyplots.git`. Vercel + Render integrations detectaron rename automáticamente sin re-link manual.
  - **(F) Backend CORS multi-origin (commit `cbac89c`).** `backend/app/main.py:25` aceptaba un solo origin via `allow_origins=[FRONTEND_ORIGIN]`. **Trade-off detectado durante setup deploy**: forzaba elegir entre "deployed prod" o "local dev" — contribuyentes corriendo frontend local contra deployed backend hit CORS errors, y Vercel previews tampoco trabajan. **Patch surgical**: parse comma-separated con whitespace trim → `ALLOWED_ORIGINS = [o.strip() for o in FRONTEND_ORIGIN.split(",") if o.strip()]`. Default sigue siendo `http://localhost:5173` (Vite dev origin) cuando env var unset — fresh clones funcionan out of the box. Production env value documentado en `.env.example` extended + README troubleshooting. Sintaxis verificada con `python3 -c "import ast; ast.parse(...)"` (uvicorn import live no se corrió). FastAPI app title también bumped de "0.0.0" → "0.2.0" en este commit (consistencia con manifests).
  - **(G) Initial deploy: Render (backend) + Vercel (frontend).** Backend: web service "storyplots" creado en Render Free tier, region Oregon (US West, matches Supabase project `mhdekknjaigoeuzrriey` xvm), runtime Python 3.11, Root Directory `backend/`, Build Command `pip install uv && uv sync --frozen`, Start Command `uv run uvicorn app.main:app --host 0.0.0.0 --port $PORT`. **4 env vars cargadas vía "Add from .env"**: `SUPABASE_URL`, `SUPABASE_ANON_KEY`, `SUPABASE_JWT_SECRET`, `FRONTEND_ORIGIN=https://storyplots.app` (sin localhost — discutido y descartado por reducir attack surface; los contribuyentes corren backend local con su propio default). **NO van a Render**: `SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY` (no se lee runtime), `SUPABASE_DB_PASSWORD` (solo psql directo), `FAL_KEY` / model keys (BYOK encriptado en Supabase Vault). Service live en `https://storyplots.onrender.com` (~3-5 min build). Health check pega `HEAD /` con 404 esperado (no hay route `/`); status "Live" igual porque puerto está bound. Frontend: project "storyplots" en Vercel Hobby, framework Vite auto-detect, Root Directory `frontend`, Install Command override a `pnpm install` (matches local), Build/Output defaults. **Application Preset alert**: Vercel detectó multi-service (frontend + backend) y sugirió preset "Services" para deployar también FastAPI — descartado por las razones SSE/persistent-process discutidas (timeouts Hobby 10s vs free Render sin timeout). Cambiado a "Vite" preset puro. **3 env vars en Vercel**: `VITE_SUPABASE_URL`, `VITE_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY`, `VITE_BACKEND_URL=https://storyplots.onrender.com` (URL Render directa por ahora — se actualiza a `https://api.storyplots.app` post Cloudflare). Production + Preview both selected.
  - **(H) Custom domain setup en progreso (no completado al cierre de sesión).** Cloudflare ya gestiona DNS de `storyplots.app` (creator pointed nameservers de Namecheap → Cloudflare durante esta sesión, propagación 5-30min típicamente). Render Custom Domain `api.storyplots.app` agregado, status "Waiting for DNS" + "Waiting for Verification". Render CNAME target: `storyplots.onrender.com`. **DNS records pendientes en Cloudflare** (todos en gris/DNS only — proxy-naranja descartado por SSE buffering risk + Vercel cert handshake): (1) `CNAME api → storyplots.onrender.com` (backend), (2) `CNAME @ → cname.vercel-dns.com` apex con Cloudflare flattening (frontend), (3) `CNAME www → cname.vercel-dns.com` (Vercel www). Cloudflare SSL/TLS mode → **Full (strict)** mandatorio; Flexible causaría redirect loops contra Vercel/Render que ya emiten certs. Pendiente post-propagation: click Verify en Render, agregar custom domains en Vercel, actualizar `VITE_BACKEND_URL` a `https://api.storyplots.app` + redeploy Vercel. **Acción pendiente del creator**: setear nameservers de Cloudflare en Namecheap (estaba en BasicDNS al inicio de la sesión).
  - **Verificación**: tsc 0 errors. Backend syntax check vía `python3 -c "import ast"` OK. Render build verde + service Live confirmado vía logs. Vercel deploy verde. Smoke test end-to-end (login + chat + SSE) **diferido** a post-custom-domain wireup.
  - **Lecciones aprendidas / catches del creator durante la sesión**:
    1. Vite no sirve estáticos desde `frontend/` raíz — solo desde `frontend/public/`. Catch durante el primer pegado de favicons (que estaban en raíz).
    2. README en línea 188 tenía clone URL pre-rename — actualizada en commit (D).
    3. Cycle 0099 inferido en gitignore: `supabase/` está gated "for now (temporary — lifted later)". README ahora explícito: schema bundle es maintainer-only para v0.2.
    4. `FRONTEND_ORIGIN=https://storyplots.app` (sin localhost) más correcto para Render que la sugerencia inicial mía. Reducir attack surface > convenience de devs corriendo frontend local contra prod.
    5. Vercel "Services" multi-service preset es un gotcha nuevo (2026 feature) — auto-detecta FastAPI y quiere deployarlo. Hay que cambiar manualmente a "Vite" o ignora silenciosamente el `backend/`.
  - **Decisiones autónomas marcadas para creator review**:
    1. **Empaquetado de 6 ejes en un solo cycle 0105** vs. cycles separados (0105 favicons, 0106 cleanup, 0107 v0.2 bump, 0108 README, 0109 CORS, 0110 deploy). Justificación: ninguno califica para cycle propio standalone (cero plan formal, todos surgical, todos parte del mismo workflow "ready for first public deploy"). Si querías traceability más granular, escalar.
    2. **`FAL_KEY` no agregado a Render** aunque pyproject.toml lista `fal-client>=0.5`. Auditoría confirmó que `backend/app/agents/fal_provider.py` recibe la key per-call (BYOK desde Supabase Vault), nunca lee `os.environ.get("FAL_KEY")`. Same para OpenRouter / OpenAI / ElevenLabs. Backend env vars list en Render: 4 SUPABASE+CORS, ninguna model-side. Si en el futuro hay un fallback model-key del proyecto (no BYOK), agregarla.
    3. **og:image apunta a `/og-image.webp` 1200×630 dedicada** (creator subió la imagen al `public/` con UUID name, renombrada). Si no querías publicar esa imagen como social-share preview, escalar — el creator puede swappearla cuando quiera y el meta tag sigue siendo el mismo path.
  - **Backlog nuevo**:
    - **Health check endpoint `/health`** — Render le pega `HEAD /` y obtiene 404 (igual marca Live porque el port está bound, pero queda warning en logs). ~5 líneas en `backend/app/main.py` o nuevo route. No bloqueante.
    - **`tool.uv.dev-dependencies` deprecation warning** en build de Render — apareció en logs uv sync. No rompe nada, lo arreglamos cuando upgradeamos `uv`.
    - **Vercel preview origins en CORS** — actualmente `FRONTEND_ORIGIN=https://storyplots.app` bloquea Vercel previews (`https://storyplots-xxx.vercel.app`). Si querés habilitar, opciones: (a) agregar regex support a `main.py`, (b) hardcodear lista expandida. Decisión post-domain-wireup.
    - **Auto-redeploy Vercel on env var change** — Vercel NO redeploya solo al cambiar env vars. Cuando `VITE_BACKEND_URL` cambie a `api.storyplots.app`, hay que click Manual Deploy → Redeploy.

- [x] **Cycle 0108 — App-feel polish: kill zoom, scale mobile, invert chrome polarity** ✅ shipped 2026-05-10 (commit `70301cb`). Plan `plans/0108-app-feel-zoom-color-invert.md`. Three interlocking visual fixes after iPhone live testing post-deploy.
  - **Viewport + base font scale**: `<meta name="viewport">` gains `maximum-scale=1.0, user-scalable=no, viewport-fit=cover` → app-feel (no pinch, no double-tap zoom, no auto-zoom-on-input-focus). `--sp-text-base 15px → 16px` doubles as iOS auto-zoom defense (16 is the threshold) AND a global ~6.7 % type bump so the UI reads native-app-sized rather than shrunk-website. Three explicit `fontSize: 15` overrides bumped to 16 (`[data-form="stack"]` inputs in `index.html`, Composer `textareaStyle` in `Composer.tsx`, `searchInputStyle` in `Characters.tsx`). MessageBubble `fontSize: 15` deliberately preserved (kit-faithful chat reading rhythm; not a focusable input — code-review F2 rejected with rationale).
  - **Mobile drawer scale**: `Sidebar.tsx` adds `isDrawer` flag plumbed to `itemStyle(collapsed, active, drawer)`. Drawer rows: icon 18 → 22, padding 0.5rem 0.75rem → 0.75rem 1rem, fontSize ~17px, gap 0.75rem → 0.85rem. Persistent desktop sidebar untouched (tight rhythm preserved for inset-card density).
  - **Chrome polarity invert** (vs cycles 0101–0104, where outer was darker `--sp-bg` and content card was lighter `--sp-bg-2`): outer flex frame → `--sp-bg-2` `#1C1C1E` on desktop, content card → `--sp-bg` `#0F0F10`. Desktop reads as a lighter chrome frame around a darker reading pane. Sidebar bg stays transparent (reads against the new lighter outer). Drawer panel lifts to `--sp-bg-2` to feel layered over the dark mobile bg. Sidebar collapse chevron (`controlStyle`) bumped from `--sp-bg-2` → `--sp-bg-3` to remain visible against the new lighter outer (code-review F1 applied — same-color blend bug). Tokens themselves are NOT edited; only where they're applied at the AppShell/Sidebar level. Internal elevation hierarchy preserved (sub-cards `--sp-bg-2` and inputs `--sp-bg-3` still elevate above `--sp-bg`).
  - **Mobile single-tone** (post creator iteration "que en mobile solo este el oscuro"): `AppShell` outer flex bg conditional on `persistent` — desktop `--sp-bg-2`, mobile `--sp-bg`. Topbar gradient `bg-2 → bg` removed; topbar reads solid `--sp-bg`. Sticky fade strip removed entirely (no longer needed since topbar bg = sheet bg).
  - **Chat invert + uniformity** (post creator iteration "creo que es el chat el que le hace falta"): `ChatShell.tsx` mobile header gradient → solid `--sp-bg`, mobile feed-wrapper bg `--sp-bg-2 → --sp-bg`, removed the chat fade strip. Desktop unchanged (already inherited the AppShell card via `transparent`). Mobile chat now reads as one continuous canvas (header + feed + composer), desktop chat sits on the dark AppShell card with a hairline border-bottom on the header.
  - **Chat fixed-feel** (post creator iteration "el header y el parte donde uno escribe esten fixed"): `AppShell` outer `height: 100vh → 100dvh` (dynamic viewport tracks iOS Safari URL bar collapse + soft keyboard so header/composer stay pinned during typing). `MessageFeed` adds `overscrollBehavior: contain` + `WebkitOverflowScrolling: touch` (rubber-band trapped inside the feed, shell does not move). Composer placeholder simplified: `"Type a message. Enter to send, Shift+Enter for newline."` → `"Type a message…"` (the longer copy was irrelevant on mobile where there is no Shift modifier).
  - **Verified L=1440×900 + S=375×812** via Playwright. Body fontSize=16 ✓, outer bg=`rgb(28,28,30)` desktop / `rgb(15,15,16)` mobile ✓, content card `rgb(15,15,16)` ✓, drawer panel bg `rgb(28,28,30)` + nav row icon 22 + padding 12px 16px + fontSize 16.8px ✓, chat header bg solid mobile / transparent+border desktop ✓, viewport meta `user-scalable=no` ✓, composer placeholder `"Type a message…"` ✓, feed `overscrollBehavior: contain` ✓, outer `height: 812px` (dvh resolved correctly) ✓. tsc 0 errors. 0 net-new console errors. Code-review: F1 applied (chevron contrast), F2 rejected (kit-faithful bubble reading-size). Code-simplifier: 0 applied / 3 rejected (drawer ternaries are tri-state, named locals document policy with ≥2 usages).
  - **Files modified** (8): `frontend/index.html`, `frontend/src/styles/tokens.css`, `frontend/src/features/shell/AppShell.tsx`, `frontend/src/features/shell/Sidebar.tsx`, `frontend/src/features/chat/ChatShell.tsx`, `frontend/src/features/chat/Composer.tsx`, `frontend/src/features/chat/MessageFeed.tsx`, `frontend/src/routes/Characters.tsx`. Non-negotiables intact (chrome-only, zero backend / schema / wire-protocol).
  - **Iteration ritual followed**: `feedback_visual_approval_before_commit.md` memory honored — paused after each visual change for screenshot review and creator OK before continuing. Three iteration cycles (mobile uniform, chat invert, chat fixed) all approved before final commit.

  - **Post-ship iPhone polish trail (2026-05-10/11)** — five follow-up commits after creator tested on real iPhone Safari + Chrome iOS exposed issues Playwright DevTools couldn't replicate:
    1. **`a503d1c` — `fix(0108): iPhone keyboard layout + drop streaming text gate`**. `100dvh` proved unstable: when the soft keyboard collapsed, the dvh value didn't always restore, leaving the composer stranded mid-screen with empty space below. Reverted to `100vh` (iOS auto-scrolls focused inputs into view inside the chat feed, so dvh isn't needed). Plus: split Composer `disabled?: boolean` from `disabledReason`. ChatShell passes `disabled={isStreaming}` silently — the typing dots are already a sufficient signal, the previous `"Waiting for the assistant to finish…"` banner undermined chat realism. Visible reasons stay only for actionable gates (rewrite, missing provider).
    2. **`2852ebd` — `fix(0108): drop conditional placeholder`**. The composer textarea's `placeholder` was switched to `"Model provider required — configure one in Settings."` whenever `gated` was true. Pre-fix that matched `disabledReason` (the model-provider message itself). After the streaming-disabled split, `gated` is also true while the assistant is replying — so the placeholder leaked the wrong copy every time the user sent a message. Drop the conditional; always `"Type a message…"`.
    3. **`dc84598` — `fix(0108): iOS web-app layout lock — full 100% chain + body fixed`**. Real iPhone showed the document itself was scrollable even with the inner AppShell `overflow: hidden` — header scrolled off, composer hid under Safari's URL bar. Root cause: `100vh` on iOS Safari is the layout viewport (constant, includes area behind URL bar) so the shell rendered taller than visible and the body became scrollable. **Fix**: full `height: 100%` chain through `html → body → #root → AppShell` plus `body { position: fixed; inset: 0; overflow: hidden; overscroll-behavior: none; width: 100% }`. With body anchored as a fixed full-bleed element, the document never scrolls — only the chat feed (or content card on static routes) has its own internal overflow. iOS auto-scrolls focused inputs INSIDE the chat feed, header + composer pin reliably. Standard pattern across native-feeling iOS web apps. Also: `apple-mobile-web-app-capable` + `apple-mobile-web-app-status-bar-style: black-translucent` meta tags for "Add to Home Screen" fullscreen.
    4. **`af566e7` — `fix(0108): composer stadium-pill shape + 16px feed-aligned gutter`**. Experimental iteration: pill `borderRadius` 14 → 999 (stadium pill, iMessage / Telegram pattern) + `composerStyle` horizontal padding 14 → 16 to match feed gutter. Creator declined the stadium shape ("no me gusta tanto pill el input") but the 16 px gutter stuck.
    5. **`4fdf39f` — `fix(0108): composer horizontal overflow on narrow phones + revert pill`**. Web Inspector on real iPhone showed the composer pill computed to **402×56 on a 375 wide viewport** — overflowing the right edge. Root cause: `composerStyle` used `display: grid` with no explicit `grid-template-columns`, so the auto column expanded to the intrinsic width of the widest child (the textarea's natural-text-width was wider than the phone). **Same bug pattern as cycle 0075 ImageViewer footer**. Fix: switch composer footer to `display: flex; flexDirection: column; minWidth: 0`. Add matching `minWidth: 0` to the pill so the inner textarea (`flex: 1 1 0; min-width: 0`) can shrink to container width. Also revert pill `borderRadius` back to `var(--sp-radius)` per creator preference. Verified live: composer width 375 (= viewport), pill width 343 (= 375 − 32 px gutter), 0 horizontal document scroll.

  - **Final files modified across the cycle** (9): the 8 from initial ship plus `frontend/index.html` was edited again for the iOS web-app layout lock. Net result: the chat surface on iOS behaves like a native app — header pinned, composer pinned, only the message feed scrolls between them; keyboard open/close doesn't break the layout; pinch + double-tap + auto-zoom-on-input all blocked at the viewport level.

  - **Patterns learned / re-learned this session** (memory candidates):
    - **iOS Safari `100vh` is the layout viewport, includes area behind URL bar** → use the `100%` chain (`html, body, #root { height: 100% }` + `body { position: fixed; inset: 0; overflow: hidden }`) for true native-app shell on iOS.
    - **`100dvh` is unstable when keyboard closes on iOS** → avoid for outer shells; rely on layout-viewport `100%` + iOS auto-scroll-into-view for focused inputs.
    - **`display: grid` with no `template-columns` and a wide-intrinsic-content child overflows on narrow viewports** → use `display: flex; flexDirection: column; minWidth: 0` instead. This is the SAME bug we hit in 0075 ImageViewer — second occurrence in this codebase.
    - **A single `gated` flag conflating visible-explanation + silent-disable causes copy leaks** (e.g. placeholder text appearing during streaming) → split `disabled` (silent) from `disabledReason` (visible) at the component API boundary.
    - **DevTools mobile emulation does NOT replicate iOS Safari URL bar behavior** → real iPhone testing is mandatory for layout-lock cycles. Playwright at 375×812 passed all gates while iPhone real failed the layout multiple times.

  - **CharacterCard image-hero redesign**: hero avatar at top with 3/4 portrait aspect ratio + rounded top corners; mode badge (`🎭`/`💬`) top-left as accent-soft circle w/ backdrop-blur; chat-count chip bottom-right (dark glass overlay, only when conversations > 0). Below image: name (1-line ellipsis), tagline (2-line `-webkit-line-clamp` + reserved `min-height: 2.7em` so rows align across cards with/without tagline — code-review F3), tags row (max 3 visible + `+N` overflow chip), time chip at bottom. Panel bg `--sp-bg-2` → `--sp-bg` so the drawer reads as a continuation of the shell rather than a separate panel — backdrop scrim provides the visual contrast. `inert` attribute applied when closed (code-review F1) so keyboard users can't Tab into off-screen nav links; `aria-hidden` alone left elements in the tab sequence.

Rejected: `MODE_OPTIONS`/`GENDER_OPTIONS` arrays (co-located + typed), `FilterChip` inline component (single call site + matches sibling `LayoutButton` pattern), CSS class consolidation (each owns distinct concern + `data-open` requires CSS selectors), per-badge style consts (single call site in same JSX tree).
  - **Verified L=1440×900**: grid `repeat(5, 227.195px)`, filterbar `position: static`, persistent sidebar untouched. **Verified S=375×812**: grid `repeat(2, 165.5px)`, filterbar `position: sticky; top: 0`, drawer panel bg `rgb(15,15,16)` (`--sp-bg`), transform `matrix(1,0,0,1,0,0)` open vs `translateX(-100%)` closed, transition `220 ms cubic-bezier(0.2,0.8,0.2,1)`, `inert` attribute on closed drawer. tsc 0 errors. Non-negotiables intact (chrome-only).

- [x] **Cycle 0110 — Email verification required before sign-in** ✅ shipped 2026-05-11 (commit `1f5b023`). Plan `plans/0110-email-verification-required-on-signup.md`. Anti-spam hardening — block unverified emails from signing in.
  - **Supabase dashboard config (creator)**: `Authentication → Sign In/Up → Confirm email` ON, `Site URL` = `https://storyplots.app`, Redirect URLs whitelist includes the prod domain `/**` + the localhost dev origin `/**`. With Confirm email ON, `supabase.auth.signUp` returns `{ session: null, user: <unconfirmed> }` and sends a confirmation email; `signInWithPassword` rejects with `error.code: "email_not_confirmed"` until the user clicks the link.
  - **AuthForm signup**: passes `options.emailRedirectTo: ${window.location.origin}/`. After successful signup, navigates to `/verify-email?email=…` instead of `/`. Supabase JS v2 with `detectSessionInUrl` (default true) auto-handles the magic-link `?token_hash=…&type=signup` query string when the user lands back on `/` after clicking — no dedicated `/auth/callback` route needed.
  - **AuthForm signin**: catches `error.code === "email_not_confirmed"` and shows a warning-bg "Email not yet verified" block with a resend pill (30 s cooldown so users don't hammer Supabase's SMTP rate limit, default ~4 emails/hour). Generic errors still flow through the existing error pill.
  - **NEW `/verify-email` route** (outside AppShell, public): logo + "Check your email" + email shown in `<strong>` from `?email` query param + resend button (same 30 s cooldown UX) + "Sign in" back-link. Matches the dark card chrome of AuthForm.
  - **Free tier compatibility**: Supabase free tier supports email confirmations with built-in SMTP (~4 emails/hour rate limit). Custom SMTP (Resend / Brevo / Mailgun free tiers) can be added later via `Authentication → Email → SMTP` if signup volume grows.
  - **Out of scope (deliberate)**: backend assert on `email_confirmed_at` (creator picked option 1 only; Supabase itself rejects unconfirmed sign-in so no unconfirmed token can reach the backend after the dashboard flip); hCaptcha at signup (marginal benefit at current low volume); OAuth provider verification (Google OAuth not currently active).
  - **Files modified** (3): NEW `frontend/src/routes/VerifyEmail.tsx`, `frontend/src/App.tsx` (route wiring), `frontend/src/features/auth/AuthForm.tsx` (signup `emailRedirectTo` + post-signup nav + `email_not_confirmed` handler + resend pill).
  - **Verified live**: `/verify-email?email=test@storyplots.app` renders correctly with email shown in strong + resend button enabled + sign-in link. tsc 0 errors. Existing flows (signin with verified email, reset password) unchanged.

- [x] **Cycle 0111 — Memory Engine: test-saved endpoint parity + Save success feedback** ✅ shipped 2026-05-12. Plan `plans/0111-memory-engine-test-saved-feedback.md`.
  - **Driver**: creator pasted an API key in `/settings/memory-engine`, clicked Update, then Test connection — and got the legacy `"Enter your current API key to test — saved keys aren't readable back to the client."` error. Save had no success banner, Test refused to verify the saved key. Creator's correct observation: the Text Engine probes its saved key without re-paste (via `POST /providers/test` in `backend/app/routes/chat.py:761` which calls `get_active_text_key` RPC against Vault). Memory Engine had no equivalent — only `POST /providers/embedding/test` that demanded `api_key` in the body. The `get_active_embedding_key()` RPC has existed since cycle 0033 (`supabase/migrations/0033_memory_rag.sql:155`, `security definer`, reads only `auth.uid()`'s row); the plumbing was there, the endpoint wasn't.
  - **Backend** (`backend/app/routes/provider_embedding.py`): new `POST /providers/embedding/test-saved` mirroring `chat.py:761` exactly. Bearer JWT only, no body. Fetches the active `kind='embedding'` row from `provider_configs` (RLS via `UserSupabase`), calls `get_active_embedding_key` RPC to decrypt the key server-side, POSTs `{model, input:"ok"}` to `{base_url}/embeddings`, parses the response dimension, updates `last_tested_ok` + `last_tested_at`. Returns the same `TestEmbeddingResult` shape as the legacy `/test` endpoint. Defensive `{ok:false, error:"no stored key"}` when there's no active row or the RPC returns nothing. ~70 lines net.
  - **Frontend** (`frontend/src/routes/MemoryEngineSettings.tsx`):
    - `onTest` now branches: when `!apiKey && existing` → POST `/providers/embedding/test-saved` with bearer only (no body); when `apiKey` is present → keep the legacy POST `/providers/embedding/test` with body. The old short-circuit `"Enter your current API key to test — saved keys aren't readable..."` branch is **removed** — it was the bug being fixed.
    - **NEW `saveOk` state** + render `<StatusBanner tone="success" testid="mem-save-result">Memory Engine updated.</StatusBanner>` after a successful upsert. Cleared on any input change (`onFamilyChange`, `baseUrl` / `apiKey` / `modelId` onChange) — the banner becomes stale the moment the user edits anything again.
    - **Microcopy update** on the API key field helper: `(leave blank to keep saved key — Test verifies the saved key from Vault)`. Makes the new behaviour discoverable.
  - **Non-negotiables (Seed §8)**: BYOK preserved (Vault is still the only place the key lives; the new endpoint decrypts server-side and uses it for a single upstream POST, never echoes it back to the client). RLS preserved (`UserSupabase` bearer JWT enforces row-scope on the select and the update). Vault encryption preserved (`get_active_embedding_key` is `security definer`, reads only the caller's row). SSE / grammar / lorebook / branching / snapshots / agent isolation untouched (settings-only).
  - **Files modified** (3): `backend/app/routes/provider_embedding.py`, `frontend/src/routes/MemoryEngineSettings.tsx`, `plans/0111-memory-engine-test-saved-feedback.md`. No migration (`get_active_embedding_key` exists since cycle 0033).
  - **Verified live**: backend booted via `dev-runbook.md` recipe; curl unauthenticated → `HTTP 401` on both endpoints (auth gate symmetric). Frontend at `http://localhost:5173/settings/memory-engine` — Save with key in input → input clears to `••••••••`, button cycles `Saving… → Update`, green banner `Memory Engine updated.` renders (screenshot from creator). Test connection step: pending creator's final confirmation message (the old error path is gone from source — verified via `grep` of the literal string returns zero hits). py_compile 0 errors backend, tsc 0 errors frontend.

- [x] **Cycle 0113 — Roleplay scaffolding defaults: author framing + slow-burn + style anchor** ✅ shipped 2026-05-12. Plan `plans/0113-roleplay-scaffolding-defaults.md`. First concrete cycle spawned from the audit roadmap (0112).
  - **Driver**: three top-line audit gaps shipped together because they share a single new settings surface and the same prompt-assembly extension pattern. Author framing (doc §2 — highest single leverage, validated by arXiv 2509.00482), slow-burn (doc §4 — replaces creator's per-character cycle 0081 SAFETY appendix with a system-level default), style anchor (doc §7.2 — depth-0 frequency-1 anti-drift, the highest-leverage anti-drift tool per the doc).
  - **Migration `0039_roleplay_preferences.sql`** (slots 0036–0038 already taken): idempotent seed of `users.preferences.rp = {author_framing: true, pacing: "slow_burn", style_anchor: true}` for existing rows that don't have the key. New users get defaults via coalesce reads at request time — they don't depend on the migration touching their row physically.
  - **Backend `prompt_assembly.py`**: four canonical text constants exported (`AUTHOR_FRAMING_TEXT`, `PACING_SLOW_BURN_TEXT`, `PACING_WARM_TEXT`, `STYLE_ANCHOR_TEXT`) — source-of-truth for both server-side injection and the Settings preview. New `substitute_placeholders(text, char_name, user_name)` helper resolves `{{char}}` / `{{user}}` / `{char}` / `{user}` (case-insensitive, whitespace-tolerant) — mirrors the frontend `substituteCardPlaceholders` regex shape. Falsy names degrade to "the character" / "the user".
  - **Prompt assembly extensions** (`build_system_prompt` + `build_chat_messages`): new Position 0 (`# Author Framing`) before the SFW block — conditions every block that follows. New Position 1.5 (`# Pacing`) between Writing Style and Character Prompt — character voice still wins on tone/lexicon while the universal gates frame relationship development. Single substitution pass at the tail resolves placeholders across every block (including user-written `system_prompt` / `scenario` that previously reached the model literal — strictly additive). Style Anchor injected as a `role:"system"` message at the end of history every turn (composes with the existing per-conversation Author's Note: style anchor sits at depth 0, then per-conv note at its own configured depth).
  - **Backend `chat.py`**: `_Bundle` extended with `rp_author_framing` / `rp_pacing` / `rp_style_anchor`. `_load_bundle` reads `prefs.get("rp", {})` with coalesce defaults. `PromptBundle` construction passes the three values through.
  - **Frontend `lib/rpPrefs.ts`** (new, ~110 lines): mirrors `memoryPrefs.ts` pattern (`loadRoleplayPrefs` / `saveRoleplayPrefs` against `users.preferences.rp` via read-modify-write). Exports the four canonical text constants verbatim from backend for the Settings preview.
  - **Frontend `routes/RoleplaySettings.tsx`** (new, ~230 lines): three sections — Author framing (toggle + preview), Pacing (segmented control off/slow_burn/warm + preview that swaps based on selection), Style anchor (toggle + preview). Each preview is a collapsible `<details>` with monospace `<pre>` showing the exact text that gets injected. Save flow + success banner ("Roleplay defaults updated. New conversations and the next turn of existing ones will use the new scaffolding.") + clear-on-edit pattern (same as cycle 0111 Memory Engine).
  - **Frontend wiring**: route added to `App.tsx` (`/settings/roleplay`). Settings index row added at the TOP of the Chat Experience group with the `Drama` Lucide icon (canonical roleplay = theater masks). Visual Roleplay icon swapped from `Drama` to `Camera` (more accurate — Visual Roleplay is image generation, not RP framing).
  - **{{char}} / {{user}} substitution semantics — important latent fix**. Pre-cycle: placeholders were resolved only in greeting (at conversation creation) and scenario display (at chat render). Post-cycle: substitution runs at backend system-prompt build time AND for any `role:"system"` content inserted into the messages array (Author Framing, Pacing, the existing per-conversation Author's Note text, the new Style Anchor). Any literal `{{char}}` / `{{user}}` reaching the model before this cycle in a user-written `system_prompt` or `scenario` now flips from "ignored or hallucinated" to "resolved correctly with the active character + persona names". Strictly additive — no regression possible.
  - **Verification**:
    - py_compile clean on both backend files. tsc 0 errors.
    - **6/6 unit-level REPL probes pass** — substitution helper across `{{char}}` / `{{user}}` / `{char}` / `{user}` / mixed-case / whitespace-in-braces / falsy-name fallback; block order (Author Framing → SFW → Writing Style → Pacing → Character Prompt); off-toggles correctly removing blocks; Style Anchor injected into messages array with substitution; warm pacing variant rendering.

  - **Deferred**: per-character override of any of the three settings; per-character cleanup of cycle 0081 SAFETY appendices (now redundant but not auto-stripped). The remaining 14 audit cycles (Refiner v2, Ali:Chat, sampler hygiene, validation gate, T1/T2/resume, hybrid retrieval, etc.) ship separately per `plans/0112-rp-quality-audit-roadmap.md`. Recommended next: **cycle 0114 — Refiner v2 anti-romance + reasoning model** to fix the character-creation drift cycle 0081 caught by hand.

- [x] **Cycle 0114 — Refiner v2: anti-romance schema instructions + reasoning toggle** ✅ shipped 2026-05-13. Plan `plans/0114-refiner-v2-anti-romance-reasoning.md`. Second concrete cycle spawned from the audit roadmap (0112). Fixes the character-creation drift cycle 0081 manually worked around per-character.
  - **Driver**: cycle 0081 documented that the refiner reliably produced romance-attractor-shaped `goals.secret_desire` ("fill the quiet space your husband left behind", "redemption", "connection through piano") on all 5 of the creator's original characters, requiring per-character manual rewrites. The root cause is in the refiner's *field-description text* in `character_refine_system.txt`: the words "secret" + "desire" attract longing-shaped content in any modern LLM's training distribution. This cycle rewrites the field descriptions with explicit anti-attractor guidance + non-romantic examples, without renaming any columns (no schema change). Pairs with a new reasoning toggle for the refiner call only.
  - **Scope narrowed vs audit's original cycle 0114**: schema-instruction rewrite + reasoning toggle ship. Deferred: separate `creation_model_override` (audit asked for it but model-validity + error handling double the surface), new `refusal_topic` + `dramatic_tension` columns (bundled with cycle 0119 validation gate), Ali:Chat `dialogue_examples` output (cycle 0116), Quick Create 5-question wizard (cycle 0118). The narrow scope is the single mechanically-verifiable win — confirm the refiner actually changes its output shape before spending cycles on UI scaffolding around it.
  - **In-flight steering note from creator** mid-implementation: *"que no por decir una cosa ya cambie, que haya un proceso de adaptacion como en la vida real… pero tampoco bloquear todo y que no haya conversacion, debe ser reactivo y parecer que es como humano tener emociones."* Caught the first draft of the rewrite which leaned too hard toward "anti-romance lock" with sweeping bans. Second draft added a preamble **"What you are trying to produce"** that explicitly says: *"They are reactive and emotionally alive. They can be moved, hurt, charmed, pleased, annoyed, intrigued, disappointed. They CAN warm up to the user — and over time, with trust and shared experience, they may come to love them. What they do not do is start there. Real connection in fiction is earned across scenes, not at hello."* Anti-flatness softened from "must include unlikable behavior" to "must surface at least one specific uneven trait or habit." The "Romance is not the default frame" rule renamed to "Relational shape ≠ romantic-shortcut shape" with explicit *"Characters are allowed to feel things about the user. The point of a roleplay character is the relationship that develops in the scenes."* What's blocked is only the **starting** shape where the character's `goals.secret_desire` is "longing for the user."
  - **Backend `prompts/character_refine_system.txt`**: ~+35 net lines. New preamble + tightened field descriptions for `personality.fears_insecurities`, `goals.secret_desire`, `goals.fears_to_overcome` with non-romantic examples + explicit failure-mode clichés to avoid ("to fill the void", "longing to be understood by someone", "barrier to love / trust issues", "secretly hopes the user will…", "yearns for someone to see the real them"). New "Anti-flatness" rule (uneven trait must surface even on all-positive input). New "Non-fabrication" rule (don't pad cards with invented romantic history). Sharpened `system_prompt` output guidance: must contain at least one explicit boundary or refusal. Sharpened `greeting` instructions: must have dialogue, must NOT pre-emptively warm "I've been waiting for you" sycophancy.
  - **Backend `agents/character_refine.py`**: extend `CharacterRefineCallConfig` with `reasoning_enabled: bool = False`. When true, payload includes `reasoning: {effort: "medium"}` + `reasoning_effort: "medium"` (mirrors `conversation.py:37-51` thinking_mode pattern — different upstream providers honor different keys; sending both is safe). Bumped upstream httpx timeout to 240s when reasoning is on (was 60s — too short for reasoning-mode latency).
  - **Backend `routes/character_refine.py`**: extend `users` select to include `preferences`. Read `prefs.character_creation.reasoning_enabled` with coalesce defaults (missing key → `false`). Pass into `CharacterRefineCallConfig`.
  - **Frontend `lib/characterCreationPrefs.ts`** (new, ~50 lines): mirrors `memoryPrefs.ts` / `rpPrefs.ts` pattern. `CharacterCreationPrefs` type, `mergeCharacterCreationDefaults`, `loadCharacterCreationPrefs`, `saveCharacterCreationPrefs`. One field today: `reasoning_enabled: bool`.
  - **Frontend `routes/TextEngineSettings.tsx`** (~+35 lines): new "Character creation" subsection inside the existing form, just after the Thinking Mode toggle. Single toggle: "Use reasoning when refining cards" with subtitle explaining the trade-offs. Save flow updated to call `saveCharacterCreationPrefs` after the existing `upsertTextProvider` succeeds — same Save button persists both. Initial load includes `loadCharacterCreationPrefs` in the parallel Promise.all.
  - **No schema change** — `users.preferences` is already jsonb. No migration. New users get defaults via coalesce reads at request time so a missing key behaves identically to a seeded one.
  - **Verified live** with three smoke passes against DeepSeek V3.2 via OpenRouter on the xvm_project: PASS 1 — Henrik Bauer thin draft (retired forensic pathologist running an antique bookshop) with reasoning OFF produced `goals.secret_desire` = *"To write a monograph on the history of forensic medicine, drawing from his own case notes…"* — zero romance attractor, perfectly anchored in his work. `system_prompt` includes the doc-required boundary AND emotional capacity ("you might slowly warm to someone who shares that depth, but you do not offer easy camaraderie"). PASS 2 — same draft with reasoning ON produced similar shape, slightly more concise (22.9s, surprisingly faster than the 63.2s non-reasoning pass) with sharper uneven edge ("former assistants found unnerving"). PASS 3 — deliberately all-positive Alex Morgan input ("kind, smart, brave, loyal, helps people, everyone loves them") — the anti-flatness rule fired cleanly: `core_traits` added *"has a sharp, uneven edge: when overwhelmed or feeling taken for granted, they become meticulously, coldly polite"*; `secret_desire` = *"To have one full day where no one needs anything from them, where they can be utterly, unproductively still without guilt or a single text message asking for advice."* — perfect non-romance, self-anchored.
  - **Files modified** (5): `backend/app/prompts/character_refine_system.txt`, `backend/app/agents/character_refine.py`, `backend/app/routes/character_refine.py`, NEW `frontend/src/lib/characterCreationPrefs.ts`, `frontend/src/routes/TextEngineSettings.tsx`.
  - **Non-negotiables**: refiner stays an isolated agent (creator-vision §7), reads only the input card + SFW flag + the new per-user reasoning preference, never reads conversation state, never writes Supabase. BYOK preserved (reuses Text Engine credentials per creator decision #4). RLS preserved. Vault unaffected. SSE / edit-as-trim / branching / snapshots / per-conv lorebook / plain-text reply path / vendor-agnostic prompts — all untouched.
  - **Code-review / simplifier**: skipped (creator decision pattern). Live verification across 3 distinct drafts confirms the rule behavior.
  - **Deferred**: model override per call (no `creation_model_override` yet — reasoning toggle alone covers the doc §3.5 recommendation when user's Text Engine is already reasoning-capable; if it isn't, a follow-up cycle adds the override). New `refusal_topic` + `dramatic_tension` columns bundled with cycle 0119. Ali:Chat (cycle 0116). Quick Create wizard (cycle 0118).

- [x] **Cycle 0115 — Ali:Chat dialogue examples** ✅ shipped 2026-05-13. Plan `plans/0115-ali-chat-dialogue-examples.md`. New `characters.dialogue_examples jsonb` (array of `{user_msg, char_reply, kind: everyday|refusal|unguarded}`). New Position 5.5 `# Voice Samples` block in `prompt_assembly.py` rendered as canonical SillyTavern `<START>\n{{user}}: ...\n{{char}}: ...` format with substitution. Refiner v2 extended to generate 3-5 entries with **≥1 refusal mandatory** per doc §3.2 — first smoke surfaced DeepSeek V3.2 ignoring the new key, fix was tightening the schema annotation to explicit "REQUIRED. 3-5 entries. MUST include at least one with kind='refusal'."
