The silence... it helps one think."*, unguarded *"The way that oak loses its leaves from the top down. My friend used to say it was showing off."* Migration `0040_dialogue_examples.sql`. Files: 8.

- [x] **Cycle 0116 — Sampler hygiene** ✅ shipped 2026-05-13. Plan `plans/0116-sampler-hygiene.md`. Audit §1.1 doc-validated RP defaults (top_p 0.95, top_k 40, min_p 0.01, freq_penalty 0, presence_penalty 0) — pre-cycle only `temperature` + `max_tokens` were forwarded. Doc explicit: freq/presence penalty MUST be 0 for character work (distort voice, break catchphrases). New `users.preferences.sampler` jsonb key (user-global; temp + max_tokens stay per-provider). `ProviderCallConfig` extended with 5 optional fields; `stream_completion` forwards non-None only. `_load_bundle` applies doc defaults at request time when key absent. NEW `frontend/src/lib/samplerPrefs.ts` (load/save/merge mirror of memoryPrefs.ts with `clamp()`). TextEngineSettings.tsx new "Sampler hygiene" subsection with 5 sliders + "Reset to RP defaults" pill. Live verified: chat round-trip payload contained `top_p:0.95 + top_k:40 + min_p:0.01 + frequency_penalty:0.0 + presence_penalty:0.0`. No migration.

- [x] **Cycle 0117 — Memory extraction in character POV + topic/significance** ✅ shipped 2026-05-13. Plan absorbed into cycle commit message. Migration `0041_memory_significance_topic.sql` adds `memory_document_chunks.topic text` + `significance smallint check 1..5 default 3`. Partial indexes on `significance>=4` and topic when non-null. `memory_search` RPC rewritten with significance boost (sig 4 = +0.05, sig 5 = +0.10) + topic boost (promise/boundary = +0.05) added to existing recency-weighted cosine score. `memory_extract_system.txt` rewritten: memories in character POV ("I" is always the character, user is "the user"); explicit right/wrong examples; new "boundary" topic alongside event/action/promise/fact/relationship; significance scale documented with default-3 + promises/boundaries ≥ 4; new "Strict source rule" anti-hallucination clause. ExtractedFact gains `significance: int` (default 3, clamped 1..5). Live verified — Inés grief-disclosure turns produced: sig 5 fact ("The user told me their sister Clara died last spring..."), sig 3 action ("I let the silence hold..."), sig 4 promise ("I offered that next week, if they like, they can tell me one thing about Clara") — all in Inés voice, no hallucinated content, significance calibrated to doc §9.8.

- [x] **Cycle 0118 — T1 character_memories (cross-conversation persistent)** ✅ shipped 2026-05-13. Audit doc §9.5 multi-tier memory architecture (T1 character-scoped persistent + T3 conversation-scoped existing). Pre-cycle: every fact lived in memory_document_chunks scoped to `conversation_id` only. Migration `0042_character_memories_t1.sql` — new table `character_memories(id, user_id, character_id, source_conversation_id, topic, significance, content, embedding, created_at)`. RLS scoped to `user_id = auth.uid()`. ivfflat cosine + B-tree on `(user_id, character_id)`. New `character_memory_search` RPC mirrors `memory_search` shape but filters by `(user_id, character_id)`. Boosts: significance step +0.08 (sig 5 = +0.16), topic in (promise|boundary) +0.07. Lower threshold for aggressive retrieval per doc §9.10. Promotion at extraction time: `significance >= 4 OR topic in (promise|boundary|relationship)` writes to BOTH T3 and T1. Retrieval per turn now runs T3 + T1 in parallel and merges by score, dedupes by fact text. Live verified end-to-end: T1 insert under user JWT (HTTP 201, RLS path), `character_memory_search` returns inserted row with similarity 0.39 + sig-5 boost 0.16 = score 0.55. Edit-as-trim preserved (T1 references source_conversation_id ON DELETE SET NULL, so trimming a conversation doesn't drop the character's memory).

- [x] **Cycle 0119 — T2 character_canon + session resume** ✅ shipped 2026-05-13. Audit doc §9.5 + §9.6. Closes the 20-turn cliff (MiniMax Talkie/Xingye research). Migration `0043_character_canon_t2.sql` — new table `character_canon(user_id, character_id PK, content, source_memory_count, generated_at)`. NEW `backend/app/agents/canon_regen.py` isolated agent (creator-vision §7) — reads T1 memories oldest-first + character name, produces 2-3 paragraph in-character prose summary. Triggered at tail of `_run_memory_extraction_task` when `(current T1 − canon source_memory_count) >= 5`. Reuses text-engine credentials already loaded for extraction. Upserts via PostgREST `Prefer: resolution=merge-duplicates`. **NEW Position 0.5** in `prompt_assembly.py`: `# Session Context` between `# Author Framing` and `# SFW`. `_load_bundle` computes gap from last assistant message; threshold 4h. When gap qualifies: builds `[Session context: It has been X since {{char}} last spoke... Relationship summary (in {{char}}'s voice): ... {{char}} has had intervening time to think... not picking up exactly where they left off emotionally.]`. Doc §9.6 critical detail honored: explicit "intervening time" caveat tells the model not to pick up exactly where the prior turn ended. Degraded version (elapsed-only) when no canon yet exists. Live verified at prompt assembly level: Position 0.5 lands between Author Framing and SFW with substitution.

- [x] **Cycle 0120 — Hybrid retrieval (tsvector entity-anchored fallback)** ✅ shipped 2026-05-13. Audit doc §9.10 — pure cosine misses entity-anchored queries when prior wording differs. Migration `0044_hybrid_retrieval.sql` — `memory_document_chunks.text_tsv` generated stored column + GIN index + `character_memories.content_tsv` mirror. Built with 'simple' dictionary (no stemming, no stop words — keeps proper nouns intact). NEW RPCs `memory_search_entity` (T3) + `character_memory_search_entity` (T1) using `websearch_to_tsquery`. Application: new `_has_entity_token()` heuristic in chat.py detects capitalized words that aren't at sentence start (excluding "I" + trivial articles). When triggered, runs entity RPC in parallel with cosine; ts_rank normalized to compete with cosine boosted scores. Free-tier Supabase fix: migration `SET LOCAL maintenance_work_mem = '64MB'` for GIN build (default 32MB was insufficient). Live verified: inserted T1 row mentioning "Clara" → entity search returned ts_rank 0.061 → normalized score 0.305.

### Summary of multi-cycle batch (0115–0120)

Closes the audit roadmap (`plans/0112-rp-quality-audit-roadmap.md`) §1.1, §3.2, §6.2, §7.2, §9.5, §9.6, §9.8, §9.10 — high-leverage list. Combined effect:

- **Cards created from now on** carry Ali:Chat voice samples (≥1 refusal) automatically + non-romance schema-instruction baseline.
- **Every chat call** now ships with doc-validated sampler hygiene + author framing + slow-burn pacing + style anchor depth-0 (cycle 0113-0114 base).
- **Memory works across sessions**: T1 persistent + T2 canon + session resume on returning users.
- **Recall is hybrid**: cosine + recency + significance/topic boost + entity-anchored tsvector fallback.

Deliberately deferred from the audit roadmap (see cycle 0112 plan):
- PList rendering (cycle 0115 in audit) — current labeled prose works, marginal token diff not worth the form change yet.
- Greeting quality nudges (cycle 0117 in audit) — mostly absorbed into refiner v2 (cycle 0114) instructions.
- Quick Create wizard (cycle 0118 in audit) — UX nice-to-have, not load-bearing.
- Soft validation gate at Save (cycle 0119 in audit) — UX nice-to-have, can ship later. The VoiceSamples component already surfaces a "no refusal yet" warning so the most critical case is covered.
- Per-character override (any of the cycle 0113 / 0117 RP settings) — per audit decision #2, user-global only for v1.
- Creation model override (cycle 0114 in roadmap) — reasoning toggle alone covers the doc §3.5 recommendation when the user's Text Engine is reasoning-capable.

**Files touched across batch 0115–0120**: 5 migrations (`0040`–`0044`), `prompt_assembly.py`, `routes/chat.py`, `agents/memory_extract.py`, NEW `agents/canon_regen.py`, `agents/conversation.py`, `prompts/memory_extract_system.txt`, `prompts/character_refine_system.txt`, `agents/character_refine.py`, `lib/characters.ts`, `lib/characterRefine.ts`, `lib/conversations.ts`, NEW `lib/samplerPrefs.ts`, `routes/TextEngineSettings.tsx`, `features/characters/CharacterForm.tsx`, `features/import/mapCardToDraft.ts`. Net code: backend ~+450 LOC, frontend ~+350 LOC, SQL ~+200 LOC.

- [x] **Cycle 0121 — Operational polish: cadence off-by-one + soft validation banner** ✅ shipped 2026-05-13. Wrap-up cycle after the QA pass + final hardening of two visible loose ends.
  - **Cadence off-by-one fix** (backend `routes/chat.py`): pre-cycle `_stream_npc_reply` counted greeting as part of `asst_count`, so cadence=3 missed `greeting + 3 turns` (4 % 3 ≠ 0 → no extraction). Now subtracts 1 from `len(asst_rows)` to exclude the greeting, so the effective trigger is "every `cadence` user-driven assistant replies after the greeting". Memory now fires on the 3rd, 6th, 9th turn for default cadence. QA pass had to set cadence=1 manually to compensate; production behavior now correct.
  - **Soft validation banner at Save** (frontend `features/characters/CharacterForm.tsx`): yellow `--sp-warning-soft` banner just above the Save button. Runs three checks against the current draft each render: (a) no `dialogue_examples`, OR no entry with `kind="refusal"` — doc §3.2 mandates ≥1 refusal sample; (b) greeting has no quoted dialogue (regex `["'][^"']{3,}["']`); (c) greeting narrates user actions/feelings (regex on second-person verbs: `you walk|feel|look|sit|stand|breathe|notice|see|hear|think|smell|sense|enter|step|move|nod|smile|frown|tense|relax`). Banner is non-blocking — title reads "Soft check — you can save anyway". Catches doc §3.4 anti-patterns at authoring time. Verified: tsc 0 errors, py_compile clean.
  - **No migration.** No schema change.

### Final state — what's covered, what's deferred, what's open

**Doc `extras/rp-character-design-knowledge-base.md` §12 implementation order (1–10 high-leverage)**:

1. ✅ Author framing (cycle 0113)
2. ✅ Character creation guidance — refiner v2 (cycle 0114)
3. ✅ Voice samples Ali:Chat (cycle 0115)
4. ✅ Slow-burn pacing (cycle 0113)
5. ✅ Style anchor depth-0 freq-1 (cycle 0113)
6. ✅ Sampler hygiene (cycle 0116)
7. ⚠️ Lorebook in character POV (cycle 0117 for memory; lorebook prose itself still keyword-matched, no POV enforcement)
8. ✅ Per-message atomic summarization (architecturally already shipped via cycle 0029 extraction pattern)
9. ✅ Cross-session T1/T2 (cycles 0118 + 0119)
10. ✅ Session resume (cycle 0119)

Items 11–12 of doc §12 (state trackers + numeric meters) deliberately deferred — doc §5 marks optional, §11 lists numeric meters as NOT-validated as a universal rule.

**Doc §10 failure modes table** — mitigated:

✅ Agree too easily (voice samples + slow-burn) · ✅ Speak for user (style anchor + author framing) · ✅ Generic feel (Ali:Chat) · ✅ Drift after 20 turns (style anchor freq-1) · ✅ Forced intimacy (slow-burn) · ✅ Forgets boundaries (topic boost + T1 promotion) · ✅ Voice flattens (freq/presence=0) · ✅ Forgets across sessions (T1 + canon) · ✅ Treats each session as first (Position 0.5 resume) · ✅ Uncanny recall (significance + message-distance fade).

Not addressable via prompt: ⛔ Moralizes / breaks fourth wall (model-level filter, requires provider switch) · ⚠️ Repeats phrases (DRY sampler not universal — OpenRouter passes it through to compatible upstreams only).

**QA pass `extras/cycle-test-report-2026-05-13.md`** ran 11 scenarios end-to-end against DeepSeek V3.2. 10/11 passed cleanly; Test 9 (session resume + full canon) had Position 0.5 fire correctly but the assistant returned an empty reply on the upper-end prompt size (DeepSeek V3.2 occasionally returns zero tokens at large prompts). Bug `_run_memory_extraction_task` referencing out-of-scope `bundle` (cycles 0118-0119 inheritance) caught and fixed live during the QA — silent failure that would have broken memory extraction for all users; HTTP responses were 200 OK while the background task threw `NameError`.

**Deferred (creator decision or low leverage)**:

- **Quick Create wizard 5 questions** (audit 0118, doc §3.4) — UX nicety; refiner v2 already internalizes the 5 questions in its prompt. Defer.
- **PList synthesis** (doc §3.1) — labeled prose vs bracketed PList is marginal token diff, no quality change. Defer.
- **Lorebook entries in character POV convention** (doc §6.2) — low impact; users rarely author lorebook entries manually, the system auto-generates memories instead.
- **Empty-reply retry/log** (QA-revealed) — operational hardening, low frequency in normal use; revisit if it becomes a pattern.
- **Per-character override of system-level RP settings** (creator decision #2 in audit) — defer until use case demonstrates need.
- **Creation model override per call** (creator decision #4) — reasoning toggle alone covers doc §3.5 when Text Engine is already reasoning-capable.
- **State trackers / numeric meters** — explicitly listed by doc §11 as NOT validated.
- **`english_style` dead field** — code cleanup not behavioral fix.
- **DRY sampler / repetition_penalty** — provider-dependent; OpenRouter passes through to compatible upstreams; not universal.

This closes the audit roadmap `plans/0112-rp-quality-audit-roadmap.md` at the high-leverage line. The system covers doc §12 items 1–10 plus the §10 failure-mode mitigations. Future iteration (UX polish, edge-case hardening, state trackers) can be picked back up per creator priority; the current state is production-coherent.

- [x] **Cycle 0122 — AI Generate from idea + creative knobs (third character-creation flow)** ✅ shipped 2026-05-13. Plan `/Users/michaelv/.claude/plans/luminous-wiggling-leaf.md` (also copyable to `plans/0122-ai-generate-character.md` for permanent local record).

  - **Verified end-to-end live**: smoke script ran 3 passes against DeepSeek V3.2 on OpenRouter:

  - **Files** (5 new + 3 surgical edits): NEW `backend/app/prompts/character_generate_system.txt`, `backend/app/agents/character_generate.py`, `backend/app/routes/character_generate.py`, `frontend/src/lib/characterGenerate.ts`, `frontend/src/routes/CharacterGenerate.tsx`. EDIT `backend/app/main.py` (router registration), `frontend/src/routes/CharacterNew.tsx` (activate placeholder), `frontend/src/App.tsx` (route wiring).
  - **Non-negotiables preserved**: generator is an isolated agent per creator-vision §7, reads only the idea + knobs + user prefs (BYOK Text Engine reuses cycle 0114's existing credentials per audit decision #4). Never reads conversation state, never writes Supabase. SSE / edit-as-trim / branching / snapshots / per-conv lorebook / plain-text reply path — all unaffected (this cycle never touches the chat path).
  - **Polish round 1 (commit `7fe5379`)** — three creator-feedback fixes bundled:
    - **Visual rewrite** via the cycle 0070 `data-form="stack"` global reset. Pre-polish issues: textarea had double border (card wrapper + own border with gap), drama card had too much vertical empty space, gender/age dropdowns used native OS styling. Fix: wrap entire form in `<form data-form="stack">` so input/textarea/select get the tokenized treatment automatically. Drop the inner-card wrapper around the textarea. Compact drama card with `display:grid + gap:0.5rem` + 4-option segmented control with `flex:1` filling the card width. Paired gender + age in a single hints card with inline selects sized via `sp-radius-sm` + `bg-inset`.
    - **"None" drama level** — 4th option for slice-of-life characters with no internal drama (friendly baker, neighbor who waters your plants, craftsperson who simply loves their work). Anti-flatness still applies (at least one specific idiosyncrasy must surface) but as a quirk, not a wound. `backstory` stays uneventful unless the seed explicitly invites otherwise. System prompt's drama_level mapping section gains the explicit "none" band.
    - **"Slice of life" tone hint** — new tone option between "Surprise me" and "Contemporary". Distinct from `drama_level=none` which is about the character's internals: `tone=slice_of_life` is about the SCENE register (everyday moments, low-stakes scenes, no genre tropes). A `drama_level=heavy` character (retired surgeon with a haunted past) can still inhabit a `tone=slice_of_life` world — scenes about morning coffee and the cat next door. Both knobs orthogonal.
  - **Polish round 2 (commit `0c418dc`)** — two follow-up UX fixes after live use:
    - **Full-page loading state.** Pre-polish: when phase=generating, the form fields stayed visible and a spinner sat below where Submit used to be — felt like only the bottom of the page was loading. Fix: when phase ∈ {generating, saving}, the whole form area is replaced with a centered loading card (55vh min-height, `--sp-bg-2` + border) holding the spinner + descriptive message + Cancel button. Header keeps the title + a small "generating…" or "saving…" indicator on the right. Clear "the whole page is waiting" signal.
    - **Auto-save after generate.** Pre-polish: generated draft landed on `/character/new/manual` with `ImportState` prefilled — the user still had to click Save to persist. After a 30-60s LLM wait, the user could think "this is done" and navigate away, losing the draft. Fix: after a successful `generateCharacter`, immediately call `createCharacter(userId, draft)` (new "saving" phase visible briefly in the loading card) and navigate to `/character/:id/edit`. The user lands in Edit Character (not Create) on a character that already exists. The button there is "Save" which now updates (not creates). If `createCharacter` fails (network, RLS, whatever), best-effort fallback to the old `ImportState` handoff so the generated draft is never lost. The form's footer Tip text updated: *"the character is saved automatically once generation finishes, and you land in the editor to refine anything by hand."*
    - **Live verified**: filled idea ("A 40s Italian fishmonger in Naples Spaccanapoli who learned the trade from his grandmother..."), clicked Generate, saw full-page loading card with spinner + descriptive message + Cancel for ~60s, then landed on `/character/63df2007-d99c-44b7-a155-4717ff1acb36/edit` with "Edit Character" title and all fields prefilled (Gianni, Neapolitan fishmonger, full system_prompt with refusal pattern for small talk + voice details). Character persists in DB + sidebar Recent Chats. Refiner output quality matches the cycle 0114 quality bar.

- [x] **Cycle 0126 — Grammar inline: live diff parity + naturalness-aware correction** ✅ shipped 2026-05-13, commit `a0cd81c`. Plan `plans/0126-grammar-live-diff-parity-and-naturalness.md`. **Bug**: live in chat the *whole* corrected sentence rendered amber; only after reload did just the changed span highlight. Cause: the SSE `correction` event carried no `original_text`, so `ChatShell` stored `""` and `diffWords("", corrected)` flagged everything. Fix: the 3 `_pack_sse("correction", …)` sites in `chat.py` now send `original_text=bundle.last_user_text`; `CorrectionPayload` (`chat.ts`) gains the field; `ChatShell` uses `ev.original_text`. **Quality**: `grammar_system.txt` rewritten so the agent also smooths grammatical-but-non-native phrasing into the natural native version that means the same thing (not just mechanical fixes), strictly preserving the user's words/intent, and the Mode B `explanation` is one concise sentence that also says *why* a phrasing sounds non-native. This aligns the prompt with the seed's existing "how it should have been said" framing (creator-vision §5.2) — the old "mechanics-only" prompt wording had drifted narrower than the seed. ⚠️ **Gotcha**: uvicorn `--reload` only watches `.py` — editing a prompt `.txt` does NOT reload the backend; restart it manually. Verified live (OpenRouter, Mode B): "help me to do this task" → "help me with this task", "I have 25 years old / live since 2020" → "I am 25 years old / have lived since 2020", already-correct messages get no correction.
- [x] **Cycle 0128 — Grammar correction-style setting (Literal vs Natural)** ✅ shipped 2026-05-14, commit `20e223a`. Plan `plans/0128-grammar-correction-style-literal-vs-natural.md`. Creator feedback: inline grammar fixes outright errors but keeps the user's literal-translation phrasing. Adds a `correction_style` grammar pref (`"literal" | "natural"`, **default `"natural"`** — = post-0126 behavior, zero regression; new key inside the `users.preferences` JSONB `grammar` blob, **no migration**). **Literal** = fix only outright errors (verb tense, agreement, spelling, punctuation, word order), keep the user's wording/structure. **Natural** = additionally rewrite grammatical-but-non-native phrasing into the idiomatic native version, same meaning. `grammar_system.txt` restructured to a style-neutral base (JSON contract + isolation + preserve-meaning rules); `run_grammar_agent` gains a `correction_style` param and appends `_STYLE_LITERAL`/`_STYLE_NATURAL` to the system prompt (before the Mode A explanation-suppression line). `chat.py` `_GrammarPrefs` gains the field (parsed with `"natural"` default), threaded through the single shared `_run_grammar_and_persist` → so the style also reaches the Reinforcement rewrite gate (creator decision: gate uses the natural rewrite — no special-casing needed). Frontend: `GrammarPrefs` type + `defaultGrammarPrefs()` + a "Correction style" radio pair in `GrammarSettings.tsx` inside the Inline card (with a note that it shapes every correction surface). **NOT the seed's "Grammar Agent Tier (Basic/Advanced)"** — that's a model-ID selector (`architecture.md §115/§203`), still an unimplemented documented gap, not bundled. Verified live L=1440 + S=375: "she continue thinking while she reach home" → Literal "She continues thinking while she reaches home" (verb fix only) vs Natural "She continued thinking until she reached home" (verbs + `while`→`until` rephrase); setting persists across reload; agent isolation preserved (only `user_text` reaches the agent — `domain.md §6 #2`). tsc + py_compile clean, 0 console errors. code-review 0 findings; code-simplifier hoisted 2 repeated style objects. ⚠️ Same 0126 gotcha applies for future prompt-only edits, but this cycle also edited `grammar.py` (a `.py`) so uvicorn `--reload` re-imported the module and re-read the `.txt` automatically. **Follow-up `polish(0128)` commit `9898708`** — the first Natural prompt only produced timid rephrases (`while`→`until`); creator clarified Natural must sound like what a native actually says, no weird/stiff phrasing. Rewrote `_STYLE_NATURAL` in `grammar.py` to be forceful (eliminate all literal-translation patterns / unidiomatic collocations, restructure freely, concrete before→after example). Verified live: "I have many years studying English but I want improve more for not sound weird" → "I've studied English for many years, but I want to improve more so I don't sound weird."

The RP scaffolding (author framing / relationship pacing / style anchor) was global-only (`users.preferences.rp`, cycle 0113) — `/settings/roleplay` literally said "Per-character overrides are not exposed in this release." This cycle adds the per-character override. **Schema**: new `characters.rp_overrides jsonb` (nullable, migration `0045_character_rp_overrides.sql` — applied manually by creator on the active Supabase `mhdekknjaigoeuzrriey`; `supabase/migrations/` is gitignored so the file is not in the commit). Shape `{author_framing?, pacing?, style_anchor?}` — any missing key inherits that key from the global; `null`/`{}` inherits everything (identical to pre-0130). **Snapshot**: `rp_overrides` added to `CharacterSnapshot` + `buildCharacterSnapshot` (`conversations.ts`) so it freezes into `character_snapshot` at conversation creation — editing the character later does not mutate existing conversations (snapshot semantics, creator-vision §8). **Backend** (`chat.py`): new pure helper `_apply_char_rp_override(char_rp, af, pacing, sa) -> (af, pacing, sa)` merges the override over the resolved global per-key; `_load_bundle` reads `char_snap["rp_overrides"]`, falling back to the live `characters` row when the key is absent (pre-0130 conversations — same pattern as `character_memory_enabled`). `prompt_assembly.py` unchanged (already consumes `bundle.rp_*`). **UI** (`CharacterForm.tsx`): new "Roleplay scaffolding" fieldset in the Settings tab — 3 tri-state `<select>`s (author framing / relationship pacing / style anchor), each with an "Inherit (…)" option showing the global value pulled from `loadRoleplayPrefs`. Helpers `patchRpOverride` (set/clear one key; clearing the last key collapses `rp_overrides` back to `null`) + `pacingLabel`. `RpOverrides` type added to `rpPrefs.ts`; `rp_overrides` on `Character` (→ `CharacterDraft` via the `Omit`) + `emptyDraft` / `mapCardToDraft` / `CharacterGenerate` initialize it to `null`. **Note — RP scaffolding is mode-agnostic**: `build_system_prompt` injects author framing/pacing/style anchor for *every* character regardless of `mode` (roleplay or assistant), so the fieldset is intentionally NOT gated on `mode === "roleplay"` (a code-review finding suggested gating it — rejected: gating would be inconsistent with the backend, which has no such gate, and with `/settings/roleplay`'s own "applies to every conversation" copy). **Verification**: tsc 0 + py_compile OK; migration confirmed via Playwright `browser_evaluate`; new conversation's `character_snapshot.rp_overrides` carries the override; `_apply_char_rp_override` covered by 7 deterministic cases (no live LLM turn — no API key in test env, but the merge feeding `bundle.rp_pacing` is fully unit-tested); UI verified L=1440 + S=375, Warm→Save→reload persists, Inherit→Save→reload→`null`; creator visual sign-off. **code-review** 2 findings both rejected with rationale (false premise — assumed a `mode` gate in `prompt_assembly.py` that doesn't exist). **code-simplifier** 0 applied (`_apply_char_rp_override` extraction already done as part of the implementation; noted optional out-of-scope follow-up: unify the `pacingLabel` ternary with `RoleplaySettings.tsx:152`). **Out of scope (decided with creator, next cycles):** wiring `characters.default_persona_id` (currently dead — `useCharacterOpen` uses the global persona), cleaning the `ChatControlsPanel` dead rows (Autopilot/AutoTTS/Debug placeholders; AutoTTS is redundant with Generation overrides), and exposing pacing inside the chat drawer.
- [x] **Cycle 0131 — Honor `characters.default_persona_id` (persona always present)** ✅ shipped 2026-05-14. Plan `plans/0131-honor-default-persona-id.md`. `characters.default_persona_id` (schema migration 0004) existed + had a "Default persona" select in CharacterForm but was **never read** — all 3 conversation-creation paths (`useCharacterOpen`, `CharacterForm.handleClose`, `ConversationSwitcher.onNew`) each called `loadPersona(userId)` (the single global persona) and ignored the character field. Also `findOrCreateForCharacter` returned an existing conversation as-is, so an old conversation created with `persona_id = null` never sent the User Persona prompt block (position 4). **Changes** (`lib/conversations.ts`): new internal `resolvePersonaId(userId, character)` = `character.default_persona_id ?? (await loadPersona(userId))?.id ?? null`; `createConversationFromCharacter` + `findOrCreateForCharacter` lost their `personaId` param and resolve internally; `findOrCreateForCharacter` **backfills** `persona_id` on an existing conversation when it is null (UPDATE of only `persona_id` — never overwrites a non-null value; "mantener fijo" per creator decision, no in-chat switcher). The 3 call sites dropped the now-redundant `loadPersona` call. `persona_id` is a mutable FK (`on delete set null`, migration 0005) — not the write-once `character_snapshot` — so the backfill doesn't trip `conversations_snapshot_write_once_trg`. **Verification** (Playwright page-context, exercises the real lib code): backfill of a null-persona conversation → DB + returned row both backfilled; new conversation for a `default_persona_id`-null character → falls back to global persona; new conversation for a character with `default_persona_id` set → that id honored; UI happy-path click works, 0 console errors. **code-review** 3 findings: **F2 applied** (`.eq("user_id", userId)` defense-in-depth on the backfill UPDATE, consistent with `listConversationsForCharacter`); **F1 rejected** (reviewer wrongly assumed `default_persona_id` is not `on delete set null` — it is; the cross-user case is already blocked by `user_personas` RLS in `chat.py._load_bundle` which reads under the user's JWT); **F3 rejected** (pre-existing greeting-block re-fetch, outside the diff). **code-simplifier** 0 changes. **ChatShell/YourPersonaCard/CollapsedUserAvatar untouched** — they keep showing the persona via `loadPersona` for feed/sidebar display; this cycle is about the persona that travels to the prompt. **Out of scope (next):** cleaning the `ChatControlsPanel` dead rows (Autopilot/AutoTTS/Debug placeholders), exposing pacing in the chat drawer.
- [x] **Cycle 0132 — Mobile sidebar: no-scroll Recent Chats + Sign out alignment** ✅ shipped 2026-05-14. Plan `plans/0132-mobile-sidebar-no-scroll-signout-align.md`. Two creator-reported drawer (`Sidebar mode="drawer"`) fixes. **(1) Sign out alignment** — two causes. (a) `UserSection`'s `rowStyle` always used the non-drawer padding (`0.5rem 0.75rem`) / gap (`0.75rem`); the nav rows + Settings use `itemStyle` which in drawer mode uses `0.75rem 1rem` / `0.85rem`. `UserSection` gains an `isDrawer` prop; `rowStyle(collapsed, drawer)` mirrors `itemStyle`'s drawer metrics. (b) caught on creator visual review — the Sign out icon was hardcoded `size={18}` while drawer nav rows use `navIconSize = 22`; the smaller icon shifted the whole row's content. `UserSection` now derives `iconSize = isDrawer ? 22 : 18` for all three icons (LogOut/LogIn/UserPlus). After both: all 6 footer+nav rows align pixel-perfect (`svgLeft 24`, icon `22×22`, `textLeft 59.59`). ⚠️ implementation bug caught by Playwright: a `replace_all` missed the sign-out `<button>` itself — fixed. **(2) No-scroll Recent Chats** — the drawer's middle `<div>` was `overflowY:auto` and `RecentChats` always rendered all 5 conversations, so on shorter phones the sidebar scrolled. The middle `<div>` is now a flex column with `minHeight:0` + `overflowY: isDrawer ? "hidden" : "auto"`; `RecentChats` gains a `fitToHeight` prop — in that mode the `<section>` is `flex:1; minHeight:0; overflow:hidden`, the row list sits in a `flex:1` ref'd `<div>`, and a `useLayoutEffect` + `ResizeObserver` measures available height ÷ rendered row height → `maxRows = max(1, floor(avail/rowH))` → slices `convs`. The list container's `clientHeight` is fixed by the flexbox (independent of row count) so there's no measure→slice→re-measure loop. Persistent (desktop L) is untouched — still `overflowY:auto`, all 5 rows, no measuring. **Verified** Playwright S=375 at 600/667/812px heights → 1/2/5 rows, nav never scrolls, footer always visible; desktop unchanged; icons aligned. **code-review** 3 findings: F1 (ResizeObserver loop) rejected — `flex:1; overflow:hidden` decouples container height from row count, `setMaxRows`-same-value is a React no-op; F2 self-rejected by reviewer; F3 (RecentChats row vertical padding ≠ nav rows in drawer) out of scope — horizontal/left alignment already matches, vertical rhythm is a pre-existing inconsistency, noted as separate polish. **code-simplifier** proposed dropping `convs` from the effect deps — **not applied**: the dep is load-bearing (the always-mounted drawer Sidebar renders before `convs` loads; without it the effect never re-runs once the row DOM mounts). Effect comment strengthened to document this.

Upload label text becomes "Uploading…" while uploading (replaces a separate side-text span). **Create mode** (`/character/new/manual`): same toolbar; the actions column shows only Upload + View reference (`AvatarGenerateControls.visible = editing && hasImageEngine` keeps Generate hidden), and the caption is correspondingly hidden — zero regression. **code-review** 3 findings: **F1 (caption always-on) confirmed intentional** — same behaviour as pre-0134, just relocated; **F2 (duplicate local `EnrichState`/`AvatarGenState` types vs module-level `*UiState`) applied** — locals removed, `useState` uses the module-level types (one source); **F3 (tablist ARIA missing arrow-key keydown) rejected** — pre-existing (roles were already on the tabs before 0134); adding the handler is a behaviour change separate from this visual cycle, noted as future a11y polish. **code-simplifier** extracted `avatarActionPillStyle` (3 column buttons shared the same 5-prop shape) and fixed a missing `boxSizing: border-box` on Generate Avatar (the other two siblings already had it). tsc 0 errors, 0 console errors, all 14+ testids preserved (`enrich-ai/cancel/success/no-engine/error`, `avatar-preview-open`, `avatar-upload-trigger/upload`, `avatar-generate/cancel/no-engine/error`, `reference-view`, `tab-avatar/info/settings`, `character-form-close`, `character-edit/create`). Verified Playwright L=1440 + S=390, edit + create modes. **Known follow-up**: tablist keyboard nav (arrow keys to move focus between tabs).
- [x] **Cycle 0137 — Seedream system prompt sync: POV / multi-subject / shot framing / group** ✅ shipped 2026-05-15. Plan `plans/0137-seedream-prompt-sync.md`. Bug reportado por creator: *"el image con third person no muestra al third person, debería incluir al user ahí en la escena"*. Investigación encontró que era síntoma de un gap arquitectónico mayor: `image_refine_system_seedream.txt` (38 líneas) **ignoraba 4 de los 9 payload fields** que `image_refine.py:_build_user_payload` le mandaba (`pov`, `user_persona`, `character_group_size`, `character_group_members`) y manejaba parcialmente un 5to (`shot_framing` — mencionaba "framing" genérico sin reglas explícitas para los 5 tags). El path Danbooru/ComfyUI (`image_refine_system.txt`, 157 líneas) sí los manejaba completamente — viola el non-negotiable de vendor-agnostic prompts del Seed (creator-vision §8). Cuando el seedream prompt fue escrito (cycle 0094), no se portó la machinery POV/multi-subject/group del Danbooru. Esa deuda quedó latente hasta hoy. **Fix:** 1 archivo (`backend/app/prompts/image_refine_system_seedream.txt`) crece de 38 → 164 líneas (+126) con **6 secciones nuevas en prosa** que traducen semánticamente las reglas Danbooru — sin escaped-parens, sin 7-slot caps, sin attention-weight syntax. Orden en el archivo: (1) **PAYLOAD FIELDS YOU RECEIVE** enumera los 9 inputs + "absent fields mean default for the simple case" para backwards-compat con el path single-subject pre-0137; (2) **REFERENCE IMAGE SEMANTICS** del cycle 0135 preservado intacto; (3) **POV & SCENE COMPOSITION** con 3 ramas — first_person OR user_persona absent → single-subject + defensive collapse para narrativa que describe el cuerpo del user, third_person + user_persona present → two-subject NEVER-DROP-USER + complementary pose si narración silenciosa + user identity sources (name → gender → appearance.* → background_story) + "no reference image for user persona" así describir identidad más concretamente + wardrobe priority + SFW extends to both + "user is IN frame, not behind camera", third_person + user_persona absent → graceful degradation; (4) **SHOT FRAMING** prose de los 5 tags canónicos (close-up = head & shoulders, portrait = crown to mid-chest, medium = waist up, cowboy = thighs up, full_body = feet to head) + reglas "NEVER close-up in two-subject" + override automático a medium_shot cuando shot_framing=close-up llega con pov=third_person+user_persona O character_group_size>1; (5) **FRAMING-AWARE DETAIL CONSISTENCY** versión light del Danbooru ("don't describe pants in close-up") + scene-required exception cuando narration explicit + note sobre WARDROBE_BASELINE applying the framing rules same way; (6) **ACTION + CONTEXT WEIGHTING (FIRST-PERSON SCENES)** verbos+props como first-class en first_person + lead the prose with action+prop + second-person camera addressing + prop precedence sobre framing suppression; (7) **GROUP CHARACTER** N members siempre visibles regardless of POV + member ordering + interactions from narrative never forced + combinatoria POV=first+group=N(no user) vs POV=third+group+persona=N+1 + no close-up in group + SFW extends to all + WARDROBE_BASELINE doesn't apply to groups (clothing per member). **Verificación live PRIMARY CASE GREEN:** Case B (Maya third_person + Roberth user_persona). Setup: POV ya estaba en third_person globally en `/settings/prompt-editor`, user persona "Roberth" honored vía cycle 0131. Flow: new conversation con Maya → mensaje "Hi Maya. I'd love to ask about the penguins..." → response in-voice ("Ja, no, good. The dive gear can wait...") → click Generate image. **Resultado:** imagen con DOS sujetos visibles — Maya (izq, cropped curly dark brown hair sun-bleached, dark amber eyes, faded blue dive polo del WARDROBE_BASELINE cycle 0135, sosteniendo coffee mug, en el porche del "MAYA'S DIVE SHOP" con cartel visible matching el scenario) + Roberth (der, mid-30s male brown hair brown shirt, mirando a Maya). Two-subject medium-shot composition natural, no close-up overshoot, identity de Maya preservada del reference_ref sterile del 0135, user persona rendered text-only sin reference image. Pre-0137 baseline habría producido sólo Maya — el bug está fixed. Screenshot `.playwright-mcp/0137-case-B-maya-third-person-with-roberth.png`. **Casos D/E/F + group diferidos** a verificación orgánica per creator priority "single ya sirve, foco en third o otras cosas" — código path cubierto, riesgo de regresión bajo. **Code-review prompt-consistency manual pass:** las 7 secciones se referencian correctamente entre sí (POV refers to GROUP; SHOT FRAMING refers to two-subject in POV; FRAMING-AWARE refers to WARDROBE_BASELINE; GROUP refers to ACTION+CONTEXT); cero contradicciones detectadas; cycle 0135 REFERENCE IMAGE SEMANTICS preservado; output JSON schema sin cambios (backwards compat con `image_refine.py:178-183` parser). **Token cost** estimado: ~2400 tokens del prompt vs ~750 pre-0137; max_tokens del response sigue siendo 600 (`image_refine.py:163`). Aceptable trade-off por 4 features completas + 1 partial fix. **Known follow-ups:** Cases D/E/F + group verification organic; si surge problema en uso real, abrir cycle de fix. - [x] **Cycle 0135 — Sterile identity reference + reduced visual weight in fal /edit** ✅ shipped 2026-05-15. Plan `plans/0135-sterile-identity-ref.md`. The `reference_ref` (white-bg half-body photo) is consumed by fal `/edit` as an IP-adapter / image-to-image anchor when chat scenes are generated — `image.py:645-685` signs a 60-min URL and passes it as `image_urls[0]`. Pre-0135, the reference photo's identity-line included `signature_style` (`lib/fal_avatar.py:_physical_attrs_line`), so the photo was generated WITH the character's signature outfit baked in (e.g., Aria with "red leather jacket" had the jacket in her reference). On fal that turned every chat scene into a model-sheet variant: same outfit, same pose, same neutral expression — regardless of narration. Verified via WebFetch against the fal.ai model API page that `fal-ai/bytedance/seedream/v5/lite/edit` does NOT expose a `strength` / `image_strength` / `denoise` / `guidance_scale` parameter to dial down the reference's visual weight — only available levers are (1) make the reference itself neutral and (2) write refiner prompts that contradict the reference more forcefully. **(A) Sterile reference prompt** (`backend/app/lib/fal_avatar.py`): 2 new constants `IDENTITY_REF_NEUTRAL_CLOTHING` ("plain white short-sleeve t-shirt, plain neutral gray pants, no jacket, no accessories, no jewelry, no hat") + `IDENTITY_REF_NEUTRAL_EXPRESSION` ("neutral relaxed expression, mouth closed, calm"). `_physical_attrs_line` gains keyword-only `exclude_wardrobe: bool = False`; when True, drops `signature_style` from the loop. `build_reference_prompt` calls with `exclude_wardrobe=True` and inserts both new tokens into the parts list (identity → neutral clothing → neutral expression → studio background → focus → style suffix). `build_avatar_preview_prompt` intentionally unchanged — preview keeps `signature_style` and user prefix. **(B) REFERENCE IMAGE SEMANTICS** in `backend/app/prompts/image_refine_system_seedream.txt`: new section inserted between intro and output schema explaining what the reference image CARRIES (face structure, body build, complexion, eye color, base hair, distinctive marks) vs DOES NOT CARRY (clothing, footwear, accessories, pose, framing, expression, background, lighting, mood). 3 MUST rules for every output paragraph: derive clothing from narration → baseline → default; derive pose/framing/expression/lighting/mood from chat moment (never from reference); always explicitly describe clothing + pose + expression + setting in the prose ("homogeneous model-sheet output is the failure mode"). Identity re-mention rule consolidated here; removed redundancy from the `refined_prompt` description. **(C) Character context block split** (`backend/app/routes/image.py:402-466`): `signature_style` removed from `PHYSICAL_IDENTITY` (now 10 fields: age/gender/build/height/hair_color/hair_style/eye_color/skin_tone/distinctive_features/voice_style). New `WARDROBE_BASELINE` block emitted ONLY when `signature_style` is non-empty (skip-if-empty). `APPEARANCE` block renamed to `APPEARANCE_NOTES` (cosmetic). Group filter (cycle 0079) ampliated to drop BOTH `PHYSICAL_IDENTITY:` AND `WARDROBE_BASELINE:` prefixes when `group_size > 1` (a group has no single signature_style). Docstring above the builder reëscrito documentando los 5 layers + precedence chain (narration > wardrobe baseline > default). **(D) Danbooru refiner sync** (`backend/app/prompts/image_refine_system.txt`): field list at section "APPEARANCE & DEMOGRAPHIC SOURCES" point 2 updated — signature_style removed from PHYSICAL_IDENTITY enumeration; new `WARDROBE_BASELINE` block annotation with the same "narration > baseline" precedence rule. **(E) Field-semantics tightening** (`character_generate_system.txt` + `character_refine_system.txt`): in-line annotations on the `distinctive_features` and `signature_style` field comments — distinctive_features is for permanent body markers ONLY (scars/tattoos/missing limbs/freckles/glasses/piercings/birthmarks/prosthetics), NEVER clothing or accessories; signature_style is the SOLE channel for clothing. Done after Hideo's live-test leak surfaced AI Generate putting "Wears a navy indigo noren-apron and a white cotton tenugui headband" into `distinctive_features`. **Verification live**: 2 test chars created in dev account `Roberth` under the new code. **Maya Okonkwo** (id `ceddffd8-c198-409f-98c2-836e4ec81ee6`, manual, marine biologist Simon's Town): preview avatar shows blue dive polo + khaki shorts contextually; reference photo shows **plain white t-shirt + neutral gray pants** sterile, identity preserved (cropped curly dark brown hair, scar on right shin, freckles). **GREEN.** **Hideo Tanigawa** (id `13371a14-9b07-4940-bb66-2d359dd4a3fe`, AI Generate, yakitori chef Beppu): signature_style correctly excluded but distinctive_features leaked apron + headband (AI Generate categorization bug, the (E) prompt edit fixes it forward; Hideo kept as-is per creator decision — not regenerated). **Subtask 4 dropped**: fal endpoint does not expose strength control, documented as inviable; switch to a model that exposes strength is a future cycle if the homogeneity persists post-(A)(B)(C). Subtask 4 finding strengthens the case for (A) — without strength control, sterilizing the reference is the only structural fix. **code-review** 2 Important findings, both pre-existing patterns: F1 `_flatten()` in `image_refine.py:113` collapses newlines in character_context (prompt-injection mitigation since cycle 0018) — WARDROBE_BASELINE label survives as inline marker, no regression; F2 image route reads live `characters` row not `character_snapshot` (gap pre-existing, my plan overstated "snapshot preserved" → corrected to "no regression"). - [x] **`fix:` ImageViewer portal — fullscreen lightbox** ✅ shipped 2026-05-14, commit `46f6961`. The image lightbox (Gallery + Chat) rendered clipped to the content card with the sidebar still visible — "se ve chocante". Root cause: the route's `.sp-page-content` wrapper carries the `sp-fade-in` animation, whose `both` fill-mode leaves a persistent `transform`; a non-`none` transform makes that element the containing block for `position: fixed` descendants, so the overlay's `inset: 0` was measured against the content card, not the viewport. Fix: `createPortal(..., document.body)` in `ImageViewer.tsx` — escapes the transformed subtree, the existing `position: fixed; inset: 0` now covers the true viewport. Context-independent (same for Gallery + Chat). ⚠️ **Latent same-bug note**: `lib/Modal.tsx` also uses `position: fixed; inset: 0` without a portal — its scrim is likewise clipped to the content card, just less visible because it's a translucent centered card. Not fixed (out of scope); portal it too if a modal's scrim coverage ever matters.

## Session 1 Gold Standard (REPLICAR en toda sesión)

> La Sesión 1 (cycles 0018–0025) fue el modelo de trabajo correcto.
> Toda sesión futura debe seguir este patrón exacto. Si un agente no
> lo replica, el usuario debe corregirlo citando esta sección.

**Cómo se trabajó en Session 1:**

1. **Planes COMPACTOS** — cada plan cabía en ~1 pantalla de scroll. El
   usuario podía leerlo y aprobarlo en menos de 2 minutos. Si un plan
   es demasiado largo, está over-scoped → dividir en cycles más chicos.

2. **Aprobación ANTES de implementar** — el plan se presentaba al
   usuario con un resumen corto en español + la pregunta "¿apruebas?".
   Sin wall-of-text.

3. **Tasks para tracking** — cada cycle usaba `TaskCreate` para crear
   3-4 tasks (migration, backend, frontend, playwright gates) y
   `TaskUpdate` para marcar progreso. El usuario veía el avance.

4. **TypeScript check constante** — `npx tsc --noEmit` después de cada
   grupo de edits frontend. Cero errores antes de continuar.

5. **Playwright gates en vivo** — cada feature se ejercía con el
   browser real contra Supabase + providers reales. No se declaraba
   "shipped" sin evidencia en la sección Verification del plan.

6. **`code-review` + `code-simplifier` SIEMPRE** — ambos corrían como
   agents paralelos al cerrar un cycle. Findings se aplicaban
   inline (bugs reales se fixeaban; nits se rechazaban con razón).
   Resultados documentados en el plan.

7. **Commits limpios** — `feat(NNNN): <short>` + body con qué cambió,
   qué se verificó, qué se deferió. Co-Authored-By al final.

8. **Ritmo: plan → build → verify → commit → siguiente** — un cycle a
   la vez, completamente cerrado antes de abrir el siguiente. Sin WIP
   acumulado.

**Lo que NO debe pasar (anti-patterns de Session 2):**

- Planes excesivamente largos que el usuario no puede revisar.
- Implementar sin aprobación explícita del plan.
- Saltear `code-review` o `code-simplifier` "por velocidad".
- No usar `feature-dev` para features multi-archivo.
- Declarar un cycle "shipped" sin Playwright gates documentados.
- Acumular cambios sin commits intermedios.

## Cycle workflow — checklist

> **Regla de compactness:** Los planes deben caber en ~1 pantalla de scroll.
> Si el usuario no puede leerlo en 2 minutos, está over-scoped — dividir en
> cycles más pequeños. Session 1 demostró que cycles de 3-5 tareas producen
> mejor código que mega-cycles de 10+. Ver "Session 1 Gold Standard" arriba.

Cada cycle no-trivial sigue exactamente esta secuencia. Claude debe trackear visualmente dónde va (TaskCreate/TaskUpdate ayuda) y marcar cada paso al cerrarlo:

- [ ] 1. **Propose** — Leer relevant Seed sections + homologous PersonaLLM-Reference. Escribir draft plan en scratchpad. Si hay >1 approach razonable, usar `AskUserQuestion` para alinear antes del draft final.
- [ ] 2. **Save plan** — Escribir a `plans/NNNN-slug.md` con frontmatter completo (`id, slug, status: draft, created`). Siempre antes de empezar a codificar. Incluye: Context · Shape · Seed sections satisfied · Commit decisions · Schema/RLS · Backend · Frontend · Verification gates · Implementation order · Critical files.
- [ ] 3. **Get approval** — `ExitPlanMode` para aprobación del creator. Proceder solo después del sign-off. (Saltar solo si el cycle es literalmente trivial per CLAUDE.md definition.)
- [ ] 4. **Implement in order — verify per subtask** — El "Implementation order" del plan enumera 3-5 subtareas atómicas, cada una con **su propia Playwright assertion** (o verify step no-UI). Implementas subtarea 1 → corres su gate → ✅ o fixeas ANTES de empezar subtarea 2. Nunca más de 1 subtarea sin verificar. Si una subtarea resulta demasiado grande, partirla en el plan y continuar. Commit único al final con todos los gates verdes — no WIP commits. Usar `feature-dev` + `serena` + `context7` según aplique.
- [ ] 5. **TypeScript check** — `npx tsc --noEmit` (frontend) limpio después de cambios frontend. Cero errores antes de continuar.
- [ ] 6. **Migrations manual** — Si hay `.sql`, escribirlo + pedir al creator que lo aplique vía Supabase SQL Editor. Esperar "listo".
- [ ] 7. **Playwright verification** — Todo cambio UI navegable se ejerce en vivo contra backend + Vite + providers reales. Marcar cada gate del plan con ✅ o detallar fallo.
- [ ] 8. **Backend verification** — Si hay cambios de backend, probar los paths críticos (endpoint curl o direct Python invocation).
- [ ] 9. **`code-review` pass** — ⚠️ NUNCA SKIP. Correr como agent (subagent_type `feature-dev:code-reviewer`). Findings van al plan `## Verification`. Bugs reales se fixean inline; nits se rechazan con razón documentada.
- [ ] 10. **`code-simplifier` pass** — ⚠️ NUNCA SKIP. Correr como agent (subagent_type `code-simplifier:code-simplifier`). Simplificaciones que reducen surface sin perder behavior se aplican. Resultados documentados en plan.
- [ ] 11. **Append Verification** — Actualizar el plan: `status: shipped`, llenar `## Verification` con outcome por gate (citar RPC response, log line, Playwright selector, etc).
- [ ] 12. **Copy plan to repo** — `plans/NNNN-slug.md` con la Verification escrita.
- [ ] 13. **Commit** — `feat(NNNN): <short>` con body que resume cambios + `Co-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.7 (1M context) <noreply@anthropic.com>`. Body incluye qué cambió, qué se deferió, qué se verificó live.
- [ ] 14. **Update SESSION_HANDOFF.md** — Tabla de cycles, arquitectura si aplica, test data si aplica, roadmap si cambió. Commit separado (`docs:`).

Al cerrar la sesión completa:
- [ ] 15. **SESSION_HANDOFF.md refleja el estado actual.** Ningún cycle shipped falta de la tabla. Tips + convenciones siguen vigentes. Plugin playbook + workflow checklist intactos.

## Cómo arrancar una nueva sesión

1. Abre Claude Code en `StoryPlots/`.
2. Dile: *"lee SESSION_HANDOFF.md y CLAUDE.md antes de empezar, luego [pedido]"*.
3. Claude debe:
   - Reconocer los cycles shipped y la arquitectura.
   - Usar el **Cycle workflow — checklist** de arriba para cualquier cycle nuevo.
   - Invocar plugins per el **Plugin playbook**.
   - Respetar seed precedence + principles de CLAUDE.md.
4. Al cerrar: **"actualiza SESSION_HANDOFF.md con los cycles nuevos y commit"**.

**Al arrancar Claude debería:**
- Saber que hay backend+frontend corriendo (o preguntar/arrancarlos)
- Entender convenciones (plans, commits, migrations manuales, Playwright verify)
- Usar los plugins instalados per el playbook
- Respetar seed + principles de CLAUDE.md
